Wang Chonghui's Speech on the National Assembly 71

Yesterday (the 1st), the National Government held a weekly memorial service for the late Premier Sun Yat-sen, and Wang Chonghui delivered a speech on the National Assembly. The following is a record of his speech:

This week, it is my turn to speak at the memorial service, and the topic is the National Assembly. First, we must know that the Fourth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang Central Committee considered convening a National Assembly to be a major and urgent issue for us at present.

Second, the late Premier's will has given us very detailed instructions regarding the future development of our country, and the will also contains a comprehensive plan, especially for convening a National Assembly and abolishing unequal treaties, and stipulates that "(it is especially necessary to urge their realization in the shortest possible time)." Although the late Premier also stipulated other plans, only these two issues were required to be realized in the shortest possible time. Therefore, we must ensure that this issue mentioned in the late Premier's will and its steps are realized in the shortest possible time.

Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, it has been working hard to abolish unequal treaties in accordance with the late Premier's will, and it must achieve its goal in the shortest possible time. This is regarding the external aspect; regarding the internal aspect,

Page 9

Excerpts of Important News 72

the issue is convening the National Assembly. The Kuomintang has paid great attention to this issue, but in the past, because society did not pay attention and warlords in various places caused trouble, the provinces were not pacified, so this major task could not be started. We can only implement this issue after suppressing rebellions and quelling internal turmoil. Some people at home and abroad do not understand the National Assembly advocated by the late Premier, and they think that the National Assembly is the same as the National Congress. In fact, these two meetings are very different. The reason why the late Premier advocated convening the National Assembly was for two purposes: First, to seek the unification of China; Second, to seek the construction of China. Therefore, we

must realize the late Premier's plan as soon as possible and convene the National Assembly. Now, the internal turmoil has been largely quelled within the shortest period of time thanks to the efforts and struggles of our armed comrades and everyone else. Now, what we must strive for is to convene the National Assembly. As I have just said, the purpose of the National Assembly is to seek the unification and construction of China. Now that China has been unified, the declaration of the Fourth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang Central Committee clearly states that the fundamental issues of nation-building will be presented to the National Assembly, hoping to unify the will of the whole country and concentrate the strength of the whole country to build China. We must not think that the National Assembly is the same as the National Congress. The late Premier stipulated in the Fundamentals of National Reconstruction that the National Congress has two meanings: one is to announce ideas, and the other is to exercise central ruling power after the constitution is promulgated. The National Assembly is different from the National Congress. The National Assembly is to solve the major issues of building China at present. The National Congress is to exercise methods and powers. The time for the meeting is after the completion of the period of political tutelage, not during the period of political tutelage. According to the Fundamentals of National Reconstruction, the National Congress will be convened after more than half of the provinces have completed local autonomy to decide on the constitution and exercise central ruling power. Our current National Assembly has a completely different meaning. If you want to understand clearly, you can further study the late Premier's declaration in 1924 and his conversation with reporters in Shanghai when he went north, and you can get a general idea. However, there is one thing that you must pay attention to. The background when the late Premier advocated convening the National Assembly at that time

was completely different from now. At that time, various places were still occupied by warlords, and the country was not yet unified, and it was still far from the period of construction. Moreover, the government at that time was in Beijing, which is very different from the current situation. Therefore, what the late Premier talked about with reporters at that time was discussing the future issues of China. The background at that time and the phenomenon of national unity today are completely different. Now that the period of political tutelage has begun, we must not interpret the words spoken in the background at that time literally when we discuss how to convene the National Assembly, how to organize it, and how to exercise it. We must study with the true spirit and form a new situation. Only if we have this true spirit to work hard can the National Assembly have the hope of success.

We must know that although the late Premier's proposition and background were different at that time, the late Premier's spirit was always the same. Although our situation today is different from the past, our spirit is also to seek to unify China and convene the National Assembly. Now China has tended to a unified situation, but there are still some invisible reactionary elements in society that can be seen. Although they do not have guns and cannons, they use some other instruments, such as reactionary remarks, to try their best to disturb society. On the one hand, they use young people as their army, and on the other hand, they cause misunderstandings among the people to oppose us. Although these reactionary elements are invisible, they are very harmful. We only have two ways to deal with them. First, we must know that the reactionary elements are misunderstanding because they do not fully understand the Kuomintang's doctrine. We only need to vigorously publicize the Kuomintang's doctrine and program to make them understand. There is another method. We must know that what they are dissatisfied with is what we have done. Regarding this point, we only need to act with conscience and do things with our hearts. We take conscience as the starting point and work hard to achieve the late Premier's spirit of "the world is for all."

Speaking of how the National Assembly will be organized and planned in the future, it needs to be decided after very detailed research. We hope that there will be a very satisfactory result when the meeting is convened. The meeting period is scheduled to be held in May next year. We hope that everyone will work hard to do it. We must understand that the National Assembly is the foundation for promoting future constitutional government and is in fact very important. This point is also something that everyone should pay attention to. During the period of political tutelage, the Kuomintang governs the country, but it is not dictatorship, and it is not like doing whatever one wants. This power of the Kuomintang to govern the country has meaning. It is the late Premier who entrusted this important responsibility to us, just like the trust system in British, American, and French laws. It is a kind of obligation. For example, if I have a very important matter that I cannot do myself for some reason, I can entrust it to a friend I trust to do it for me. Another example is that someone entrusts their will to a lawyer to execute it. Therefore, this is due to the trust of the entrusting party, not the right. Our responsibility is very great. Our great responsibility is to exercise power on behalf of the people through the trust of the Kuomintang. This is called the Kuomintang governing the country. We all hope that everyone can work hard to do it so that we will not be condemned by our conscience when we hand over this great responsibility when constitutional government begins in the future.

We have been gradually carrying out the abolition of unequal treaties instructed to us in the late Premier's will, and we are about to achieve success. And the National Assembly will also open in May next year. Recalling that it has been five years since the late Premier entrusted us with that task, it has taken five years of hard work and struggle to achieve today. Although the late Premier did not stipulate the shortest period for future work, we must also work harder to complete the late Premier's great mission of "the world is for all." This is what I hope for everyone.

Lifting of Martial Law Announced in Ganzhou 73

In the future, public security will still be the responsibility of the garrison headquarters. Nanchang Correspondence: The bandit communists Zhu De, Mao Zedong, and others advanced into Nanxun via Yongfeng, Xingan, and Zhangshu in July. Zhu's forces even advanced to Fengcheng, 120 miles away from the provincial capital. In order to consolidate the rear, Lu, the commander-in-chief of the Ninth Route Army, specially appointed Zhang Huizan, the commander of the 18th Division, as the temporary martial law commander of Nanchang and promulgated martial law regulations to implement martial law. Since then, all the entertainment venues in Nanchang City have been closed, and from 9:00 p.m. to dawn every day, no one is allowed to walk on the road without a password. The city scene suddenly became bleak and desolate. The bandit-occupied counties on both sides of the Gan River were gradually recovered, and the air in the provincial capital improved day by day. The financial situation in the market also gradually improved. Commander-in-Chief Lu specially telegraphed Xiao, the Chief of Staff of the Ninth Route Army, on November 29, ordering that martial law be lifted from today (the 1st). All the entertainment venues are therefore reorganizing and preparing to open. It is found that the tension in the province since the declaration of martial law on July 26, four months and six days ago,

has gradually disappeared. The garrison headquarters' announcement of lifting martial law is recorded below: (According to the telegram from Lu Yan, the commander-in-chief of the Ninth Route Army of the Punitive Expeditionary Force, all the bandits have been repeatedly defeated by our army and have now fled far away and will no longer endanger the provincial capital. It is ordered that martial law be declared lifted from December 1st. In the future, the public security of Nanchang City will still be the responsibility of the garrison organs. In addition to reporting and distributing, it is hoped that the citizens will be notified for information, etc. According to this, Nanchang City is an important place in the provincial capital. I am sincerely afraid that communist bandits and hooligans will mix among them and take the opportunity to think about their success. In order to strictly prevent the treacherous and wicked, a password pass is still required to pass through the streets after 12:00 p.m. In addition to reporting and ordering, the public notice will be issued so that everyone knows. This notice (the 1st).)

Hubei Provincial Government Announces the Huang Changgu Embezzlement Case 74

The case of Huang Changgu, the former Director of the Construction Department of Hubei Province, who used excessive funds during his tenure, has now been thoroughly investigated by the Hubei Provincial Government. The results show that there is indeed embezzlement. In addition to submitting a request to the central government to dismiss and punish Huang, the entire case was also announced yesterday. The Provincial Government's announcement is recorded as follows: (It is found that Huang Changgu, a member of this government, handled a total of 1,875,079 yuan, 7 jiao, 4 fen, and 8 li of old and new receipts during his tenure as the Director of the Construction Department. In addition to borrowing and transferring 300,000 yuan to the Finance Department and paying 150,000 yuan to the central government, the remaining 1,425,079 yuan, 7 jiao, 4 fen, and 8 li was not only used up completely in just over half a year, but also required an additional 240,000 yuan for the completion of the fortress roads.

There were many abuses and no achievements. As a result, public opinion condemned him and the Kuomintang criticized him. At that time, Cheng Jun was on the front line

punishing the rebels and felt heartbroken when he heard about it. Later, it was reported that the former director of the department had withdrawn all the public funds deposited in the Hubei Provincial Bank when the military situation on the front line was tense, and it was not known what his intention was. Therefore, the committee of this government designated members Zhang Guanshi, Xiong Bingkun, Xie Lvfang, Da Zhi, and Secretary-General Hua Jueming to be responsible for investigating the accounts and projects handled by the former director in order to verify and handle them. The former director was afraid of guilt and repeatedly evaded. He first secretly went to the capital and claimed that he was going to Liuhe to meet with the Commander-in-Chief to report on the fortress road project, and telegraphed that all the documents had been submitted directly to the central government. He then submitted a request to be transferred to Beijing for review. After telegraphing a request to the National Government, he was still allowed to investigate locally by this government and has found conclusive evidence and obvious cases of corruption, exceeding 50,000 yuan; over-budget and improperly reported expenses, over 14,000 yuan; unauthorized use of funds, nearly 600,000 yuan; and the total number of pages and accounts of his handled account books were inconsistent with the number of pages and accounts of the sub-accounts, which is a clear proof of complete fabrication. Cheng Jun, as the supervisor, was responsible and dared not conceal it. He had already submitted the documents to the Chairman of the National Government for review when he went to Beijing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang Central Committee. After returning to the province, he telegraphed the Executive Yuan to order Huang Changgu to return to Hubei immediately to handle the handover of duties. Now, according to the verbal report of the members of the Fortress Road Acceptance Committee, the numbers of the Hanzhoung, Zuozhen, Cangyang Roads accounts did not match between the numbers issued by the department and the numbers received by the engineering office, and the numbers issued by the department did not match the numbers received by the contractors. The whole situation was chaotic and the abuses were obvious. The piers of the Fuhe Bridge he repaired were already tilted and would collapse in the spring flood. The foundation of the Houhu Road, which cost over 30,000 yuan, was hasty and erroneous, and the road was completed but could not be used. Once the water rose and washed away, it would turn into nothing. And the high unit price of the entire road was even more shocking. And according to the proposal of Member Xie Lu, in order to jointly investigate and verify that the evidence of Huang Changgu's, the former Director of the Construction Department, inflated reports and indiscriminate expenditures was conclusive, please announce the entire case immediately and submit a request to the National Government to first remove the member from his position and severely punish him in accordance with the law in order to clean up the officialdom. The 75th meeting of this government decided to announce the entire collection immediately and report it to the central government. In addition to investigating and deciding to submit a request to the Executive Yuan to promptly remove the former director from his current position as a member of this government, order him to return to Hubei immediately to liquidate and punish him severely in accordance with the law, and wait for the completion of the acceptance of the Fortress Road Provincial Highway before reporting and announcing separately, the attached report on the investigation of the Huang case and its evidentiary photos are hereby urgently attached for public notice. (The report on the investigation of the Huang case is omitted due to space limitations))

Liaoning Province Plans to Establish a Match Monopoly Bureau 75

Shenyang Correspondence: Zhang Zhenlu, the Director of the Department of Finance of Liaoning Province, previously stated that since matches are a daily necessity for society, the demand in various parts of Liaoning Province is very large. Although there are many domestic match factories in this province, only four companies, such as Guandong Sanming, Zhengsheng, and Huilin, have relatively large capital and wide sales channels. However, in recent years, due to the oppression of Swedish match merchants, all have suffered a setback. Small factories have mostly been bought by foreigners, resulting in the formation of a Swedish merchant monopoly on matches in Liaoning Province, and the outflow of profits is enormous. In order to resist foreign merchants and recover rights, it is proposed to establish a Match Monopoly Bureau. All matches from domestic factories in this province are not allowed to be sold by the factories themselves. All matches will be purchased and sold by the bureau to resist foreign goods. A request has been submitted to the Provincial Government to be forwarded to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee for review. Now, an order from the Political Affairs Committee has been received stating that this case has been approved by this meeting. The proposed establishment of a Match Monopoly Bureau by the Department should be approved for trial implementation, and the Department of Finance of Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces should follow suit. After receiving the order, the Department of Finance of Liaoning Province considered that the establishment of a Match Monopoly Bureau was urgent and specially decided on the following implementation measures: (1) Investigate the number and names of match factories in Liaoning Province; (2) the

total amount of capital of each factory and the location of establishment; (3) the annual

sales volume and where they sell best. Once these are ascertained, the establishment will be implemented immediately. A letter has been sent to the General Chamber of Commerce of each province yesterday to instruct the Match Industry Federation to comply with the investigation to facilitate preparations (the 29th).

Zhenjiang Express News 77

The Construction Department of Jiangsu Province telegraphed that the second conscription of labor for road construction in various counties of Jiangsu Province should be started on December 1 throughout the province. The counties that have started construction are Jiangning, Liuhe, Jurong, Kunshan, Qushan, Suining, Muyang, Rugao, Huai'an, Tongshan, Xiaoxian, Pixian, etc., a total of 23 counties. Zhenjiang is scheduled to start construction on the 10th of this month, Liyang on the 15th, Funing on the 20th, and other counties such as Taicang, Xinghua, and Gaoyou, etc., a total of 21 counties, have reported active preparations.

The Provincial Training Department had previously sent personnel to various counties together with the Construction Department to guide the organization of people's organizations and has completed the task. Now, Yu Huaizhong and Tan Peiyan have been sent to guide the organization of central counties in Lianshui, Muyang, Huaiyin, Siyang, Huai'an, Suqian, Quying, and Gaoyou counties. Huaiyin is the central county. Zhang Renjie is guiding the organization of central counties in Nantong, Rugao, Haimen, Qidong, and Chongming counties. Nantong is the central county. Lu Baolin is guiding the organization of central counties in Taixian, Funing, Taixing, Dongtai, Xinghua, Yancheng, and Jingjiang counties. Nantong is the central county. All the instructors have set off to convene meetings with the training ministers of each county in the central county.

Xu Enzhao, the County Magistrate of Peixian, was dismissed by the Provincial Government for using counterfeit currency, and the director of the county's public security bureau was secretly ordered to detain Xu for investigation. Yu Bingxun, the successor, took office today.

The Zhenjiang-Danyang section of the Zhenjiang-Guangdong Road was originally scheduled to start construction yesterday. However, due to the incomplete list of conscripted workers, it has been postponed to the 10th of this month.

The Zhenjiang Inland River Wheelboat Bureau has been competing with each other since last year, reducing fares and increasing the number of services, resulting in considerable losses. Yesterday, the Chamber of Commerce and the Shipping Association came forward to mediate and resolve the issue. It was decided that from now on, the Heban Zhenqing (Jiang), Zhenbao (Ying), and Zhenyou services will operate once a day upstream and downstream. Each wheelboat bureau will operate on a rotational basis, limiting

each service to one wheel and one barge. The fare shall not exceed the previous amount. A joint office will be set up by each wheelboat bureau to manage the boat tickets, and the remaining profits will be divided equally according to shares (December 2).

Overseas Chinese in London Organize the Chinese Businessmen's Association 78

London Correspondence: The number of overseas Chinese doing business in the UK has been increasing year by year. However, there has always been a lack of organization. Recently, the leading overseas Chinese businessmen in the area, in view of this, have initiated the organization of the London Chinese Businessmen's Association. More than 30 overseas Chinese businessmen have joined. The purpose of the association is purely to protect the interests of Chinese in the UK and to help Chinese who come to the UK. The association will do its best to help Chinese who come to the UK, whether they are studying, doing business, or traveling. According to the association staff,

the association has received and assisted many Chinese who have come to the UK in the past few months, and has made great efforts to assist and guide Chinese workers in the UK. The articles of association were adopted when the association was established (the current chairman of the association is Lin Bingrong, the executive committee member and honorary treasurer is Li De,

(Bank of China, London), the executive committee member and honorary secretary is Xi Zhizhen, and the secretary's address is 128/130 Shaftesbury Avenue, London Wi.

If you have any inquiries, you can send a letter to the above address). The following is an excerpt: (Article 1) Name: The name of this association is the London Chinese Businessmen's Association. (Article 2) Purpose: (A) To enhance the reputation of China and Chinese people abroad; (B) To strengthen the friendship between all members; (C) To enhance the interests of overseas Chinese businessmen in Jiangsu; (D) To promote Sino-British commerce; (E) To improve understanding between the people of China and the UK and other countries outside the UK. (Article 3) Staff: (A) Honorary President; (B) Honorary Vice-President; (C) Chairman; (D) Treasurer; (E) Secretary; (F) The chairman, treasurer, and secretary of the executive committee are ex officio members of this committee. (Article 4) Election of Staff: The executive committee members and other staff shall be elected by the members at the annual general meeting. The annual general meeting shall be convened by the secretary in January of each year. (Article 5) Membership: Members shall be divided into the following three categories: (A) Full members: Any Chinese who has been or is currently doing business or other professions in the UK may become a full member of this association. However, full members have the right to vote at general meetings and special meetings. (B) Associate members: Any Chinese who has other professions or is in other places may be elected as an associate member. (C) Any person from China who

comes to the UK for travel may be elected as a travel member. (D) Any new member should be proposed by a member of the executive committee, seconded by a member, approved by all members of the executive committee, and passed by a majority of the members present at the meeting. (E) The quorum for meetings of the executive committee is three people. The quorum for meetings of members is one-quarter of the members. However, only full members have the right to vote at annual general meetings and special meetings. (F) The executive committee shall convene a meeting in the shortest possible time upon receiving a request from eight members. (Article 6) Membership Fees: (A) The initial 40 full members who join the association shall pay a membership fee of £2 and 2 shillings per person per year. Members who join after the 40th member shall pay an initial membership fee of £1 and 1 shilling per person. (B) Associate members shall pay an initial membership fee of £1 and 1 shilling upon joining and an annual membership fee of £1 and 1 shilling per year. (C) Travel members are not required to pay membership fees, but they may be asked to donate freely. (D) Members who join the association in the first half of the year shall continue to pay the full-year membership fee, but those who join in the second half of the year shall pay only half of the membership fee. (E) Any member who delays payment of fees for two months may have their membership revoked by the executive committee after three months unless the member has a legitimate reason. The committee may revoke the membership of any member whose actions hinder the motherland and the association. The committee has absolute power over this matter and its disposal is deemed appropriate. (Article 7) Amendment of the Articles of Association: The articles of association may be amended with the consent of more than half of the full members at the annual general meeting or special meeting. (Article 8) Duties of the Executive Committee: The executive committee shall host the following duties: (A) Hold monthly social gatherings; (B) Visit scenic spots and industrial and commercial areas; (C) Hold industrial and commercial discussions and lectures; (D) Strengthen ties and cooperation with associations of the same nature in China; (E) Enhance the interests of overseas Chinese businessmen through visits or social gatherings; (F) Pay attention to news and facts about China and Chinese people in newspapers, publications, movies, and dramas and take appropriate action at any time; (G) Enhance the feelings of Chinese and British people through gatherings and other methods; (H) Participate in or cooperate with other groups that promote world peace.

Nanhui 79

Detailed Report on the Fire in Zhoupu Town: At 9:15 p.m. the day before yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out in the Lu Tonghe Basket Shop next to the Second Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau on Zhuhang Street in Zhoupu Town. Although the town's Fire Brigade rushed to put out the fire with a western-style fire engine, the fire was so fierce that it was difficult to extinguish, resulting in the burning of the two-story building in front of the Second Sub-Bureau (containing one five-shot quick-firing gun, two nine-shot Mauser rifles, one pistol, and dozens of rounds of ammunition used by the police, which could not be retrieved and were also destroyed), Shen Yongji's Palm Bed Shop, Kang Xingxing's Woodworking Yard, Sanxing Car Shop across the street, Lu Tonghe's Workshop, the residences of Ji Jingen and others, Tang Ai's Ready-Made Clothes Shop, and Chen Yingchang's Basket Shop. The fire was finally extinguished at 10:00 p.m., destroying more than ten buildings, totaling 28 two-story and one-story buildings, with losses estimated at more than 30,000 yuan. An elderly woman and a girl in Lu Tonghe's shop were also burned to death. It was learned that the cause of the fire was that Lu Laifu, the owner of Lu Tonghe's shop, had a quarrel with his wife and threw a kerosene lamp on bamboo flowers. Because the shop was full of utensils, all of which were flammable, it was difficult to save the situation once it caught fire. Lu Laifu has been arrested by the Second Sub-Bureau and presented to the Public Security Bureau for transfer to the county for interrogation. Robbery and Murder Outside the West Gate: At the house of Zhu Shuzhou, a resident of the 97th Tu outside the West Gate, more than ten robbers suddenly came to rob last night. When Zhu Shuzhou heard the alarm, he quickly held a tool and went outside, intending to sound the gong to gather the crowd to resist the robbers. However, he was spotted by the robbers, who shot and killed Zhu. They then entered the room and searched, stealing gold ornaments, silver dollars, and other items, with losses estimated at more than 300 yuan.

Framed Accusation and Sentencing; Cai Bosong, a Former Staff Member of the Fourth District Office of Yangzhong County and Current Township Chief of Renli Township, Had a Grudge With Shi Xieyang, the Chief of the Fourth District; He Forged a Document From the District Office, Privately Used the Seal, and Engraved Shi Xieyang's Private Seal, Falsely Accusing Zhao, the Section Chief of the Second Section of the Civil Affairs Department; Lu Yong and Huang Che of the Civil Affairs Department Discovered This During Investigation and Reported It to Director Hu, Who Ordered the Yangzhong County Government to Summon Him; After the Trial Member Peng Yigu Compared the Handwriting in Court, It Was Confirmed That It Was Written by Cai Bosong; The Seal Used on the Official Document Was Stolen From a Blank Document That Had Already Been Sealed, and the Stroke and Ink Color of the Private Seal Were Also Inconsistent With the Case Submitted by Shi Xieyang; His Crime of Forging Official Documents Was Confirmed; The County Government Sentenced Cai Bosong to Imprisonment for One Year and Two Months and Deprived Him of Public Rights for Three Years as a Warning.

Qingjiang 88

Huai'an Money Shop Was Robbed; Four Bandits Went to Rob Dingyixiang Money Shop in Duozi Lane, Huai'an City; At That Time, the Shop Clerks Suspected That They Were People Exchanging Silver Dollars and Did Not Think That They Were Bandits; Unexpectedly, After the Four Bandits Entered the Shop, They Closed the Shop Door, Took Out Guns From Their Sleeves, and Threatened the Shop Clerks to Not Make a Sound; Then, One or Two of Them Watched Over the Shop Clerks, While the Rest Searched and Robbed a Total of More Than 500 Yuan; At That Time, Public Security Police Yin Debiao and Others Were on Patrol and Apprehended a Bandit Named Zhang Suizhi; They Took Him to the Bureau for Interrogation and He Confessed That His Accomplices Were Hiding in the Xiaokezhan Inn Behind the Huaian Customs Office in Banzha; The County Government Sent Cavalry Police to Continue Apprehending Zhang Xueshu and Lu Mou, 15 Miles Away From the City in Banzha Town; They Were Taken to the City and Sent to the County Government for Handling.

Nanjing 89

Buddhist Painting Exhibition Scheduled to Open; The Lay Buddhist Forest Has Been Preparing for the Buddhist Painting Exhibition for Many Days; Now, We Have Received News From Shanghai That Lay Buddhists Qian Huafu and Zhu Shiseng Will Bring Buddhist Images to Beijing in the Near Future; The Exhibition Is Scheduled to Open to the Public in the Forest on the 6th of This Month; It Is Said That There Is Also a Buddhist Image Inscribed by the Late Premier; Also, Dharma Master Chi Song Was Greeted by the Lay Buddhist Forest Yesterday; Bao Yin, Xie Jin, Chen, Zhou Zhongliang, Wei Gangchang, Mei Xieyun, Liu Lingsheng, Zhang Xiaolou, Xu Fohang, and Other Great Lay Buddhists Attended, Making It a Grand Occasion.

Huzhou 90

The Xixiang Kidnapping Case; Zhu Jinsheng, a Farmer in Zhuangwuli, About Thirty Miles Outside the West Gate of Changxing, Had Some Property, Which Was Coveted by Bandits; On the Night of the 29th of Last Month, More Than Twenty Bandits Suddenly Came, Each Carrying Guns, and Broke Down the Door and Searched at Will, Robbing All Clothes and Ornaments; Before Leaving, They Kidnapped Zhu's Youngest Son; Also, a Farmer Min, Who Rented and Cultivated Fields in Yangxitan, Outside the East Gate of Changxing, Made a Living by Working Hard; On the Same Day, More Than Ten Bandits With Guns and Wooden Sticks Suddenly Broke Down the Door and Robbed Clothes and Bedding; The Bandits Went to Min's Neighbors and Robbed Four Families in a Row, With a Total Loss of About 300 Yuan; Also, Gao, a Villager in Sanwu, Near Yangxi, Had a Modest Family Fortune and Was Coveted by Bandits; At About 6:00 PM on the Same Afternoon, Four Bandits With Wooden Shell Guns and a Henan Accent Broke Into His Home and Robbed Extensively for About Half an Hour Before Firing a Gun as a Warning and Leaving.

Xiaoshan 91

The Village Chief of Tianjing Village Was Kidnapped; More Than Ten Bandits Suddenly Came to Miao Jiakun, the Village Chief of Tianjing Village in Southern Xiaoshan, on the Night of Yesterday; They Crossed the Wuchengling Ridge From the Border of Zhuji and First Destroyed the Gate Before Robbing Extensively; All Clothes and Ornaments Worth About 500 Yuan Were Robbed; In Addition to This, Village Chief Miao Was Kidnapped; Before Leaving, They Left a Letter Stating That Someone With a Red Hat Should Negotiate the Ransom at the Wuchengling Border Within Ten Days, Otherwise They Would Tear Up the Ticket.

Yancheng 92

The Notorious Bandit Cai Wanlin Was Killed; Since Li Mingyang, the Director of the Provincial Security Office, Came to Yancheng to Supervise the Suppression of the Bandits, Ma Niyu Ren Has Already Fled, but His Evil Deeds Are Still Causing Trouble in the Countryside; The People Are Suffering Unspeakable Hardships; Recently, Cai Wanlin, a Notorious Bandit in Dongxing Township, the Second District of the County, Was Searching in the Countryside With His Flag; Qiu Baohua, the District Chief of the District, Supervised Cai Xiufeng, the Head of the First Regiment, to Arrest Cai Wanlin and His Concubine Cai Boshi and His Accomplice Zhang Changsong; Unexpectedly, Chen, a Member of the First Regiment (It Was Heard That Sun and Cai Were in the Same Gang), Privately Released Cai; District Chief Qiu Baohua Sent Cai Boshi, Zhang Changsong, and Chen, the Regiment Member Who Privately Released Cai, to the County for Legal Action; He Then Arrested Cai Wanlin at Night and Killed Him on the Spot; It Was Heard That Cai Was an Important Officer Under Ma Niyu; Now That He Has Been Killed, the Luge Area in Southeast Yancheng May Be Able to Obtain Some Stability.

Liuhe 93

The Bandit Forces in the Northwest Have Become Rampant Again; Since the Northwest of Liuhe Borders Lai'an and Other Counties in Anhui Province, Bandit Troubles Have Frequently Occurred; After the Garrison Command Sent Teams to Conduct Suppression, the Counties of Lai, Lai'an, and Tianliu Were Stable for Several Months; Recently, Bandit Gangs in Lai'an Have Risen Up, With Reportedly Twenty-Three Gangs; Each Gang Has Thirty to Fifty People; They Come and Go Without a Trace, and the People Are Suffering; Kidnapping and Extortion Are Occurring Almost Every Day; It Was Recently Heard That Merchants in Liuhe County Who Went to Lai'an to Collect Debts Were Intercepted by Bandits; Four Livestock Were Lost, and Three People Were Kidnapped; Each Person Required 500 Yuan to Be Redeemed.

Educational News Highlights

Wang Jingqi to Be President of Labor University 94

Nanjing, 2nd - Today's Executive Yuan meeting resolved to appoint Wang Jingqi as President of Labor University.

Yang Lian Appointed Director of the Social Education Department of the Ministry of Education 95

Yang Lian, Director of the Social Education Department of the Ministry of Education, returned to Shanghai from abroad the day before yesterday and reported everything to Minister Jiang in Beijing. Because he had been away from home for a long time, he had to return to his hometown to visit his family, so he was unable to officially take office at the department. He returned to Hangzhou and officially took office as Director of the Social Education Department of the Ministry of Education yesterday. Chen Shizhen, who was concurrently serving in the department, has clearly handed over all the political affairs in the department.

Jiangsu and Hubei Provinces Request to Change Academic Qualifications 96

The Ministry of Education Found It Difficult to Approve; Principals of Jiangsu Provincial Primary and Secondary Schools and the Fourth Middle School in Hubei Province Requested That the Education Departments of Their Respective Provinces Ask the Ministry of Education to Change the Academic Qualifications Promulgated by the Ministry of Education, as They Were Quite Obstructive; The Ministry of Education Instructed the Education Departments of Jiangsu and Hubei Provinces Yesterday, Saying That It Had Received the Report; The Prohibition of the Use of the Old Calendar and the Implementation of the National Calendar Has Been Clearly Ordered and Complied With by the National Government; All the People of the Country Should Abide by It, and All Levels of Schools Should Earnestly Promote It to Set an Example and Benefit Implementation; The School Winter Vacation Is a Disguise for the Old Calendar New Year Holiday, Which Has Been Clearly Disclosed in This Ministry's Order No. 293 and Abolished; It Is Not Allowed to Exist; Although There Are Inevitable Difficulties at the Beginning of the Reform, All Levels of Schools Should Still Uphold the Revolutionary Spirit and Strive to Implement It and Should Not Request to Change the Regulations Because of Inconvenience; The Teachers and Principals of All Schools Should Be Instructed to Understand This Meaning; This Is Essential.

American Smith Sends a Team to Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou to Collect Specimens 97

The American Smith Institution Organized an Investigation Team to Investigate Animal Specimens in Yunnan and Guizhou Provinces and Requested the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Issue Passports; The Education Department and the Academia Sinica Carefully Formulated All the Organization and Procedures of the Team; Yesterday, the Education Department Consulted the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Issue Passports; The Following Is a Description of the Measures Agreed Upon by the Team and the Academia Sinica: (1) Route; Maoping, Sichuan Province, Is Located North of Yazhou and Is the Most Important Area for Collecting Specimens in Western China; At the Same Time, in Order to Collect Complete Specimens of White Bears for Dissection and Several Kinds of Antelope Specimens for Installation, It Is Necessary to Go to the Mountains North of Donghe and Stay for Some Time, or Go to Wasi Territory Northwest of Chengdu; If the First Two Items Can Be Collected Quickly, We Should Go South to Xuzhou, Through Northern Yunnan, and Enter Guizhou Province; Around June of Next Year, We Will Return to Nanjing to Meet With the Academia Sinica to Review and Organize the Specimens Before Packing Them and Transporting Them to the United States; (2) Collection Personnel; Smith and Six Chinese Assistants, One Photographer, One Representative for Reporting, Two Specimen Installers, and One Trainee Installer; (3) The Academia Sinica Appointed Director Qian Tianyuan to Negotiate With Smith and Establish the Following Restrictions: (A) All Collected Specimens Must First Be Transported to the Museum of This Institute; Only After Being Reviewed by Experts Hired Can They Be Transported Abroad; (B) This Institute Will Send One or More Collectors to Participate; (C) After the Specimens Are Reviewed by Experts, A Complete Set Must Be Retained in China.

Jiangsu Provincial Scout Instructors Held a Joint Oath-Taking Ceremony 98

And Opened a Discussion Meeting With Important Proposals (Zhenjiang Correspondence); The Jiangsu Provincial Training Department Convened Scout Instructors From Various Counties to Hold a Joint Oath-Taking Ceremony in the Auditorium of the Provincial Party Headquarters Yesterday; Cao Minghuan, Zhang Yuanyang, Secretary Yu Huaizhong of the Training Department, Chen Bangcai, Scout Instructor of the Province, and 49 Scout Instructors From Various Counties Attended; Cao Minghuan Chaired the Meeting and Reported the Significance of the Meeting; It Was Decided That Chen Bangcai Would Report the Current Situation of the Scouts in Various Counties Before the Oath-Taking Ceremony Was Held; After the Oath Was Taken, the Supervisor Zhang Yuanyang, the Witness Cao Minghuan, and Secretary Yao of the Education Department Gave Speeches Successively; Yu Huaizhong Gave a Speech at the End; The Oath-Takers Gave a Reply; Then, a Photo Was Taken and the Ceremony Was Completed.

At 2:00 PM in the Afternoon, the Instructors Held a Joint Discussion Meeting; The Important Proposals Are as Follows: (1) Presenting to the Jiangsu Provincial Party Consolidation Committee to Send a Letter to the Education Department to Determine the Funding Standards for Scout Activities in Jiangsu Province to Facilitate Development (A) Establishment and Recurring Expenses of County-Level Primary and Secondary School Corps (B) Establishment and Recurring Expenses of Provincial Experimental Primary School Corps (C) Recurring and Temporary Expenses of the Council (2) Requesting the Provincial Consolidation Committee to Amend the Interim Regulations on the Treatment of Scout Instructors in Various Counties to Make Full-Time Employment the Principle; Full-Time Branch Cadres Should Receive a Living Allowance; Part-Time Employees Should Receive a Horse Allowance According to the Original Amount (3) Requesting the Provincial Consolidation Committee to Continue Training Scout Cadres.

Record of the Jiangsu Normal Education Achievement Exhibition 99

This Jiangsu Provincial Normal Education Achievement Exhibition Was Held at Yangzhou Middle School; More Than Ten Schools With Normal Science and Rural Normal Science Departments From Various Provinces Participated, and the Achievements Were Extremely Rich; The Number of Visitors Was Exceptionally High, and the Sheer Number Was Overwhelming; Among Them, the Manual Achievements of Huaiyin Middle School's Normal Science Department and the Design Achievements of a Small School in Yangzhou Were the Best; The Achievements of the Rural Teachers Were the Richest at Jieshou Rural Teachers; Their Self-Made Physical Instruments and History and Geography Manual Achievements Were Extremely Suitable for the Rural Environment and Full of Educational Meaning; The Achievements of Other Schools Were Also Dazzling and Extremely Beautiful; The Contribution to Normal Education Was of Great Value.

Party Doctrine Essay Speech Competition

Middle School Essay! Deadline on the 20th

Primary School Speech! Preliminary Round Scheduled for the 10th

(National Society) The Shanghai Municipal Party Committee's Training Department Is Organizing a Party Doctrine Essay Competition for Middle School Students and a Party Doctrine Speech Competition for Primary School Students in Order to Encourage Primary and Secondary School Students to Study Party Doctrine. County Education Bureau Orders Schools to Collect Tuition Fees 101

The Shanghai County Education Bureau Issued an Order to All Levels of Schools Yesterday, Saying That the Case Was Submitted for Discussion at the 65th General Affairs Section Meeting Held by the Bureau on November 28th. How to Investigate and Settle the Case of Collecting Tuition Fees by Month on a Trial Basis in Each School This Semester Is About to End. It Was Decided (In Addition to Ordering Each Education Committee to Investigate the Actual Number of Receipts School by School During the Third Inspection and Report to the Bureau, a Notice Should Be Sent to Each School Principal to Be Responsible for Collection and a Letter Should Be Sent to Each District Office for Investigation) to Strictly Collect to Increase Revenue and Fund Settlement.

Progress of the Chinese Social Science Association 102

The Chinese Social Science Association Was Founded by Yang Youjiong, Zhang Yuanruo, and Other Famous Scholars in Our Country Three Years Ago. The Association's Address (Namely, the Publishing Department) Is Located at No. 38, Lane 1603, Jing'an Temple Road in This City. Its Main Purpose Is to Promote the Cultural Movement of Science in Order to Save the Decline of the Academic World in Our Country in Recent Years. It Has Been Working Hard for Several Years and Has Made Significant Progress. Recently, It Has Been Making Even More Progress. The Following Is a Summary of Its Situation:

(1) The Sharp Increase in Membership; The Members of the Association Are All Scholars at Home and Abroad, Such as Kong Qingzong, Xu Fu, Ling Menghan, Ling Jihan, Chen Zhenzhi, and Ruan Changqiu; There Are Now More Than 100 Members; It Is Also Planned to Establish Branches in Beijing, Guangzhou, London, Paris, New York, Japan, and Nanyang; It Can Be Organized in the Near Future;

(2) The Rapid Progress of Publishing; The Association Publishes Two Journals: One Is the Social Science Magazine, Which Has Now Been Published to Volume 2, Issue 5, and Sells More Than 10,000 Copies Per Issue; One Is the Social Science Movement, Which Has Been Published to Issue 39; The Former Is Published in Shanghai and Has Been Changed From a Quarterly to a Monthly; The Latter Is Published in Nanjing and Has Been Changed From a Semimonthly to a Weekly; Recently, It Has Been Actively Seeking to Develop the 8th Issue of the Social Science Magazine; The Duguit Special Issue Is More Dedicated to Modern Legislative Issues; The Attitude Is To Strive for Purity and the Proposition Is To Strive for Correctness in Order to Become the Center of Social Opinion; It Is Heard That the Association's Publishing Department Also Plans to Compile the Chinese Social Science Association Series, the Social Science Series, and the Social Science Foundation Series; On the One Hand, It Seeks to Contribute to Specialized Academics; On the Other Hand, It Seeks to Popularize Social Science Among the General Public;

(3) Emphasizing Social Work; The Association Also Believes That the Previous Work Focused on Propaganda and Neglected Practical Service Work; It Is Planning to Establish a Social Science Academy to Provide Young People With Opportunities to Study Social Science; In Addition, It Is Planning to Establish a Social Science Bookstore and Library;

Jida Education Department Visited Huangdu Rural Teachers 103

In Addition to Emphasizing Theoretical Discussion, the Education Department of National Jinan University Also Emphasizes Practical Observation; Therefore, the Educational Places Along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Are Almost All Visited; The Day Before Yesterday, Dr. Shao Shuangqiu, the Head of the School, Personally Led the Third and Fourth Grade Students to Huangdu to Visit the Shangzhong Rural Normal Department; Dr. Huang Jingsi, the Director of the Department, Led Them to Visit All Places for a Week; Then, They Discussed the Current Issues in Rural Education in the Auditorium; Dr. Huang Was Also a Lecturer in the Department, So He Felt Especially Close; He Also Invited Them to Lunch; The Dining Hall Was Posted With Slogans Such as "One Bowl Is Not Enough, Two or Three Bowls Are Just Right" (Everyone Does Things Together, Everyone Eats Together); The Slogans Were Concise and Artistic, and the Vegetables and White Rice Were Especially Rural in Flavor; After the Meal, All the Teachers and Students of the Department Held a Welcome Meeting and Invited Dr. Shao to Give a Speech; Dr. Dengtai Stressed That Labor and Education Are One; Schools and Society Should Not Be Separated; The Development Is Thorough and the Audience Clapped Constantly; They Also Praised the Department's Teaching Policy and the Teachers' and Students' Efforts; Then, Lian Bingsong, the Student Representative of Jida University, Thanked Them for Their Hospitality; After the Meeting, They Visited the Department's Experimental Primary School and Kindergarten and Discovered Many Practical Difficulties in the Current Rural Schools; After Returning to School, They Plan to Study Separately to Find a Solution to Contribute to Society.

Anniversary Celebration of the Re-establishment of the Wusong Merchant Marine School 104

The Wusong Merchant Marine School of the Ministry of Communications held its anniversary celebration of its re-establishment yesterday, the 30th. Although it was a rainy day, the guests still arrived enthusiastically. The Ministry of Communications specially sent Cai Pei, Director of the Navigation Administration Department, to participate in the grand ceremony. Other prominent figures from the shipping industry and education sector, such as Yuan Ludeng, Hu Shuhua, and Ou Yuanhuai, also arrived at the school one after another. The meeting commenced at 10:30 AM, presided over by Yang Ying, the acting principal of the school. After formal salutations, the history of the school and the state of affairs of the school's re-establishment anniversary were reported. Next, Cai Pei, the representative of the Ministry of Communications, delivered a speech. Subsequently, Hu, Ou, Yuan, and others gave speeches one after another, encouraging the youth to cultivate naval talent and revitalize the shipping industry. Finally, representatives of the faculty and students gave replies. The ceremony concluded at approximately 12:00 noon with a group photo. In the afternoon at 4:00 PM, the school held a grand entertainment program with over twenty performances. Wang Qingxun's performance of "Heaven and Hell" and "Little Serenade," as well as the joint performance of "Fen He Wan" by Peng Zhongli and Xu Houjun from Jiaotong University, and the joint performance of "Sitting in the Palace" by Yan Zhenyu, a teacher at the school, and Zhang Mingde, a guest, were all outstanding. The event ended at approximately 11:00 PM. It was also reported that the school's land and water sports meet, originally scheduled to continue the next day, was postponed to this Friday due to rain.

Establishment of the Dongtai Fellow Provincials National University Alumni Association in Shanghai 105

In recent years, there have been many students from Dongtai County studying at various national universities in Shanghai. However, due to being scattered in different areas, there was little opportunity for interaction and communication. Recently, it was heard that the Education Bureau of the county intends to cancel subsidies for various national universities. Feeling the need for unity, Fei Jun of Jinan University and Liu Peikun of Labor University initiated the organization of a National University Alumni Association of Dongtai Fellow Provincials in Shanghai. A founding meeting was held a few days ago, and Jin Nianzu of Jinan University, Liu Peikun of Labor University, and Yuan Baodong of Jiaotong University were elected as executive committee members. In addition to planning considerable discussions on the exchange of knowledge, Liu Peikun was also appointed as the standing committee member to actively handle the registration of members from various universities who have not yet joined the association and matters related to the Education Bureau's subsidies.

Charity Basketball Games in Memory of Zhao Shiming: Hua Team Wins One, Loses One 110

(1) Women's Group: Liangjiang defeats West Girl's YMCA

25 to 16

(2) Men's Group: Mixed team loses to Pirates

44 to 25

The Chinese and Western charity basketball games in memory of the late basketball star Zhao Shiming were held last night at the China Basketball Stadium. With the four teams being elite forces, the competition was expected to be highly entertaining, so guests flocked to the stadium, filling it to capacity. As a result, the Liangjiang women's team defeated the West Girl's YMCA 25 to 16, and the Chinese mixed team lost to the West Qing Pirates team 44 to 25. A brief account is given below.

Thanks to Players and Guests 111

As the game was about to begin, Hao Boyang, a leading member of the Association for Advancement, entered the court and first thanked the players and spectators. He said that he was deeply grateful for everyone's participation in the game or for making a special trip to watch. The proceeds from the tickets would be donated to charitable organizations in memory of Zhao Shiming.

Liangjiang defeats West Girl's YMCA 112

Overall View: After Hao Boyang finished speaking, the two women's teams began their contest. Xi Jun, the center of Liangjiang, opened the scoring with an extremely agile move, breaking the basket with a pass from Shao Jinying. Xi Jun continued to score, and in the first quarter, Liangjiang took a 6-2 lead. Subsequently, the West Girl's YMCA scored three points with three consecutive free throws. Shao Jinying retaliated, and Liangjiang won the first half 9-5. In the second half, the West Girl's YMCA made some changes, but due to Liangjiang's close monitoring, they still could not improve. Xi Jun showed great skill, and the final score was 25 to 16. Referee: Shu Hong.

Team Performance: Liangjiang's performance was commendable. No one was more agile than Xi Jun, and Shao Jinying was a flexible forward. The best of the defenders were Zhuang, Wang, and Yang Ren. The talent of the defenders as forwards was only seen as a lack of strength, and too much back-and-forth passing led to missed opportunities, which was a pity. The West Girl's YMCA had courage but lacked strategy. The turning techniques were not yet mastered, and inaccurate shooting was a major problem.

Mixed Team Loses to Pirates 113

Great Momentum: After the women's group, the two men's teams began to compete. Initially, the Chinese mixed team had great momentum. Although Smith first scored a long shot, the Chinese center Wei Haiqing countered with a steal and scored, and Wei scored again, immediately surpassing the Pirates. However, Smith's probing shots were incredible, and he scored thirteen points in a row, while the mixed team only had six points.

Enemy Rampant: The mixed team requested a timeout and then fought again. The enemy's momentum was still unstoppable. Nu Chao was fierce and unstoppable. Smith and Shia responded to each other and created a score of 18 to 6. Kong Guangyi entered the game, and the situation eased slightly. The Pirates won the first half 22 to 8.

Slight Shift: In the second half, the Pirates' three forwards were still fierce. Although the mixed team replaced Li Chengyuan with Tan Da and changed to a defensive strategy, the Pirates' momentum was still rampant. Until the score became 34 to 11, the mixed team's three forwards Tan, Liang, and Wei scored four points in a row, making the score 34 to 19. In the end, the wind was small and the strength was weak, and it was useless.

No Way to Save: Just hoping for a turnaround, Sullivan lurked like a tiger, and the five Pirates players came one after another. There was no way to save the situation. The Chinese mixed team lost 44 to 25. Referees: Zhang Guoxun, Wanfu. The mixed team's defeat was due to the fact that they gathered temporarily and lacked coordination, and they only focused on offense without paying attention to defense, allowing Smith and others to sweep the entire court, which was a pity.

Ping Pong Champagne Cup Finals News 114

(1) After the Shanghai Race Club Members' Club announced the Ping Pong Champagne Cup Finals news, people from all walks of life flocked to obtain tickets, creating a scene reminiscent of the road to Shanyin. However, the Cup Competition Organizing Committee, due to the limited space of the Ningbo Fellow Provincials Association, in order to maintain order, the number of tickets prepared was not large. The distribution of tickets was also regulated. Each team participating in the Cup Competition was given ten tickets, and all others were declined. However, there were still those who wanted to obtain tickets as an exception, which was difficult to grant. The committee asked for understanding from all sectors. In addition to Zhao Fang Photo Studio and the club, Chen Shaofeng, the director of the Association of Fellow Provincials at the North Railway Station, is now also entrusted to sell tickets so that those who wish to watch the ball game can purchase them nearby. According to the rules of the Ningbo Fellow Provincials Association, tickets cannot be sold on site, so tickets will not be sold at the time of the competition. Spectators are advised to prepare them early to avoid a wasted trip.

Chamber of Commerce of Shanghai Asks to Prepare for Year-End Closing 115

To the Chambers of Commerce of Provinces, Cities, and Counties: The Chamber of Commerce of Shanghai telegraphed on the 1st, saying: "We, the Chambers of Commerce of all provinces, cities, and counties, have been repeatedly ordered by the Executive Yuan and our municipal government to investigate and deal with the year-end closing of the national calendar, considering it a key measure for promoting the national calendar. Previously, according to the requests of various industries, we suggested extending the deadline to the day before the Beginning of Spring, but the Social Affairs Bureau rejected this proposal in detail at each level. This approval has also been published in various newspapers in this city. It can be generally seen that it is imperative. Recently, however, we have received telegrams from various chambers of commerce, all of which suggest that our chamber is still arguing for an extension. This shows a lack of clear understanding of the government's purpose of actively promoting the national calendar, leading to this divergence of opinions. Furthermore, the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce recently proposed to extend the deadline to February 16th, the date of the completion of grain transportation, as the date for the closing of accounts. However, this proposal was collectively discussed by the 39 chambers of commerce of Jiangsu Province and submitted to the central and provincial governments for approval and implementation. Currently, this case has not been formally approved by the central government. Therefore, it is currently difficult to adopt the extension to the completion of grain transportation. There are very few days left until the legal closing date, and various chambers of commerce and industries may still hold on to this wait-and-see attitude. We are deeply concerned that the result of procrastination may affect the market and accounting firms. Therefore, we are specifically telegraphing to declare that we hope to immediately inform businesses to prepare within the year and avoid any further hesitation. This would be greatly appreciated. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce East."

Holiday Dates for Foreign-Owned Factories 116

Should Be Handled the Same as Chinese Factories: The Ministry of Foreign Affairs informed the ambassadors and chargés d'affaires of various countries the day before yesterday, conveying the instructions of the Executive Yuan to all foreign-owned factories. Hereafter, foreign-owned factories shall observe the dates stipulated by the Executive Yuan for worker holidays and handle them the same as Chinese factories, without discrimination. The embassies of various countries have already notified the manufacturers to take note.

Overseas Chinese Chambers of Commerce in British Colonies Jointly Request Cancellation of the Provisional Passport Law 117

The Chinese Overseas Association received a letter yesterday from the Chinese General Chambers of Commerce in Singapore, Penang, Malacca, Selangor, Perak, Kuala Lumpur, Muar, Bentong, Kuantan, Mentekab, and other ports, stating: "Our chambers of commerce have jointly submitted a document to the National Government, saying: 'We respectfully report that after the Ministry of Foreign Affairs promulgated the Provisional Measures for Issuing Passports for Leaving the Country and Issuing Passports for Returning to the Country by Overseas Embassies and Consulates, overseas Chinese groups at home and abroad have felt distressed and have fiercely opposed and striven for their repeal. Our joint association, after investigating the flaws in the two measures, has listed several points for reference and has raised the reasons for petitioning for their cancellation as follows: (1) The passport fee is six yuan per passport and the stamp duty is two yuan. Those who leave the country without a passport will not be protected. Passports were originally intended to prove nationality so that our embassies and consulates abroad could provide protection in accordance with the treaties. Why should additional fees be charged? The situation of overseas Chinese is also different from ordinary inspections, investigations, travels, and businesses. Our people are troubled by food and clothing or suffer from various disasters, and there is no room for them in the interior. Those who bear to leave their parents, wives, and children and flee to foreign countries are all doing so out of desperation. Their travel expenses are either borrowed or begged for, or even obtained by selling their property and children. How can they bear the heavy burden of additional expenses in such a dire situation? This is not feasible, point one. (2) Applicants for passports for leaving the country should first fill out a form for applying for a passport for leaving the country. Applicants for ordinary passports should also submit a request letter along with the following guarantee documents and submit them to the passport issuing authority for approval. Those leaving the country to do business should submit a guarantee letter from the local chamber of commerce or two reputable firms and certify the amount of their capital. Those leaving the country to work should submit a guarantee letter from the local labor union or two reputable firms and certify their work skills. Most overseas Chinese leave the country because of poverty or are driven by local communists. They have no belongings of their own. How can such poor people obtain a guarantor? It is difficult to find a small shop, let alone two reputable firms. Such a method makes it impossible for the poor to live and forces them to die in ditches. The strong ones become bandits. This is not feasible, point two. (3) Collecting passport fees for returning to the country is the same as for leaving the country. Overseas Chinese suffer various harsh regulations in various countries, such as entry taxes or head taxes, but the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has not been able to alleviate their suffering. Now, it wants to collect a return passport fee of eight yuan when overseas Chinese return to their country. The external department calls it protection, but the overseas Chinese view it as an increase in taxation. This is not feasible, point three. (4) Replacing passports and paying taxes every year. Although countries generally have procedures for citizens to apply for passports for leaving and returning to the country, there is no precedent for replacing passports every year. Now the external department has stipulated replacing passports every year, and its intention is only to collect fees every year. What crime have overseas Chinese committed to be subjected to such heavy exploitation? This is not feasible, point four. (5) Applicants for passports for returning to the country should have their passport at the time of leaving the country inspected before being approved for issuance. Overseas Chinese may have left the country decades ago or before the promulgation of harsh regulations and have not obtained a passport. How can they have a passport to be inspected? Such a method directly aims to prevent overseas Chinese who left the country without a passport from having any way to return. This is not feasible, point five. The above five points are only the most extreme and cruel ones. There are other difficult places to implement that are difficult to list. Our government upholds Sun Yat-sen's legacy and aims to abolish unequal treaties with foreign countries. Why hasn't there been any reduction in the harsh regulations of the host country, but harsh regulations for overseas Chinese to obtain passports for leaving and returning to the country have appeared first? The two measures for applying for passports have no effect on the protection of overseas Chinese. It is simply the Ministry of Foreign Affairs calculating that with the number of overseas Chinese leaving the country exceeding one million annually and the number of overseas Chinese residing in various countries exceeding ten million, if they all comply with the measures for obtaining and replacing passports, the government will have tens of millions of yuan in revenue each year. However, it does not consider that overseas Chinese who flee the country have no way to return, and those who are oriented towards the country have no way to enter. What is the meaning of the Principle of People's Livelihood? What is the meaning of protecting overseas Chinese? Our joint association believes that these two measures are closely related to the interests of our overseas Chinese and cannot remain silent and allow the devastation of harsh chapters and tyrannical regulations. Moreover, the Chinese General Chambers of Commerce and various overseas Chinese groups in the Malay Peninsula have sent letters and telegrams one after another, loudly calling for and vowing to strive for the cancellation of the two measures for leaving and returning to the country. We humbly request that the National Government approve and order the external department to withdraw its order to comply with public opinion. This would be a great act of kindness. Respectfully submitted to the Chairman of the National Government, Chiang Kai-shek. Singapore Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, Penang Chinese Chamber of Commerce, Malacca Chinese Chamber of Commerce, Selangor Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, Kuala Lumpur Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, Muar Chinese Chamber of Commerce, Bentong Chinese Chamber of Commerce, Kuantan Chinese Chamber of Commerce, Mentekab Chinese Chamber of Commerce."
