News from Trade Associations 166

Rice and Grain Industry: Fan Hesheng, Chairman of the Shanghai Rice and Grain Trade Association, sent a letter to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday, requesting it to forward a letter to the Banking Association, stating: "Respectfully, regarding the case of Maoye Bank banknotes, although the one-yuan notes have been cashed, there has been no news of cashing for the five-yuan and ten-yuan notes. Our colleagues have a considerable number of these notes, which are vital to their capital and difficult to turn around. The end of the lunar year is approaching, and the impact on finance is by no means insignificant. Many banks in Shanghai issue banknotes, and the Banking Association should bear the responsibility of safeguarding credit. If it does not supervise and recover the Maoye banknotes, the commercial sector will suffer a profound impact. To avoid harm, it is inevitable that everyone will tend towards cash transactions. Once this prediction unfortunately materializes, the impact of hindering finance will make the entire commercial sector feel uneasy. Judging from the news that dozens of banks in the United States have recently collapsed, this unfortunate news is indeed alarming to the world of commerce. For the sake of commercial security, we are specially requesting your esteemed association to forward our request to the Shanghai Banking Association to find ways to urge the Maoye Bank Liquidation Office to redeem the five-yuan and ten-yuan banknotes to maintain credit and ensure commercial stability. Sincerely, the public enterprise." Addressed to: Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce.

Tea Industry: The Shanghai Nanshi Tea Trade Association encountered a major dispute among its members due to the case of Wanfeng Yongfasheng violating industry regulations. Repeated meetings failed to resolve the issue. Yesterday, it convened an executive committee meeting again. Prior to the meeting, it sent a letter to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce requesting it to send representatives to the meeting for guidance and invited Zhou Lutang, the owner of Wanfeng Yong Store, to attend together. The meeting was held at 2 PM yesterday. More than ten committee members attended, chaired by Cao Xiujun. (1) Greetings as usual. (2) Reporting the purpose of the meeting. (3) Announcing the reasons for the Wanfeng Yong's case and asking for public discussion and resolution. It was resolved to handle the case in accordance with the various regulations stipulated in the association's charter. Zhou, the owner of Wanfeng Yong Store, also understood the situation deeply and said that in this era, various industries cannot exist without the maintenance of industry regulations and organizations. Therefore, he voluntarily accepted the resolution. After the representative of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Jin Shengbai, certified the resolution, Zhou Lutang signed it to indicate his agreement. The meeting adjourned at 6 PM.

Acknowledgement: We thank the Bank Weekly for gifting us a copy of Bank Weekly, No. 677, yesterday.

Weather Report 167

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The Yangtze River basin is cold and clear, the Shandong coast and south of Ma'anshan are overcast, with northwest to northeast winds of varying degrees along the coast of the country. Also, yesterday at 3 PM, the highest temperature in this city within 24 hours was 49.1 degrees, and the lowest was 28.4 degrees. On the same day last year, due to drastic climate change, there were no recorded highs and lows.

Letter 168

To the Editor: In your newspaper's local news on the 30th of last month, there was a report about the Jiangda ship being damaged in Xun, which is inconsistent with the facts. According to our bureau's investigation, the Jiangda ship departed from Shanghai on the 21st of the previous month and arrived in Xun on the morning of the 25th to dock and unload cargo. No accidents occurred. On the same day, it safely arrived in Hankou at midnight. This week, when sailing downstream 12 kilometers above Jiujiang, due to the rudder malfunction, it could not avoid colliding with the shore. Only one or two iron nails in the anchor chain cabin were loosened, causing minor leakage. However, there was absolutely no water entering the cargo hold. This concerns the reputation of the bureau's ship. We hope that you will disclose this letter in the local news column and offer our best wishes. Addressed to: Shenbao News Agency. Sincerely, Secretariat of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company General Administration, December 2nd.

Incoming Correspondence

Humble Suggestions on Promoting Pure Silk National Goods for Lake Products for Clothing Materials by Zhu Tanru 169

Since the world's commercial war, our country has been invaded by foreign goods. Patriotic people have been advocating national goods as a solution. However, many people talk about it, but few act on it. One reason is that they admire the beauty of foreign goods, and the other is that there are no national goods to replace them. Take the mandarin jacket as an example. Anyone in society who has even slight social interaction has one. Now, fancy silk satins have become a thing of the past, and wool and serge are extremely fashionable. If we calculate one-four-hundredth of our country's 400 million people, approximately one million people wear mandarin jackets. Each jacket costs ten yuan, totaling ten million yuan exported in one year. Other men's and women's long and short clothes are many times more than this. It is truly sad to say. Now, pure silk mandarin jacket material from Lake products has been invented, which is commonly known as crepe de chine. It is dyed black, has a luster without floating light, and has no creases even when pressed. If satin is used as the lining, it feels even more elegant. It is cheaper and better than wool serge. Ordinary stores do not yet have this product. It is said that the largest silk stores in Shanghai, Hangzhou, and Huzhou already sell this crepe. You can try it and know that this statement is credible. I serve in the Lake City and care about the silk industry. Based on my conscience, I offer this bitter advice. Rather than empty talk about promoting national goods, why not actually try and use them? I hope that all patriotic gentlemen in the country will pay attention to it. It would be fortunate if they do not disregard it because of my insignificant position and words. Zhu Tanru, Wuxing Unified Donation Collection Bureau, November 29th.

Free Talk

A Word of Wisdom 170

— Yimei

In a degenerate age, seeking morality is harder than finding a spring in the desert.

Vulgar soil prefers to write articles, and ugly women prefer to apply powder.

Feelings must be close to infatuation to be genuine, and talent must be close to interest to be transformative. This is what a wise man said, and I deeply admire it.

Going to the field of love is like going to the battlefield. You must be brave and energetic to win.

People like to dance and drink wine, but I like to brew tea in the bamboo forest.

Adorning a beautiful flower on a beauty's head is not considered a waste.

The presence of clouds in the sky is like a bathing woman wearing thin silk, covering her mystery.

In turbulent times, theorists take those who keep silent as their role models.

Men of letters do not like to show their original drafts, just as women are unwilling to show their faces without makeup.

Only extraordinary people can create works that lament the world and pity people in a world of bright lights and wine.

Those who are disappointed in love are most afraid of listening to love songs.

Talented women rarely have beautiful and charming appearances.

When chatting with those who do not share the same values, one often racks one's brains and finds no topics to talk about.

Lying in a warm quilt and listening to the howling wind outside, one often has the idea of building a big house to shelter scholars.

Paying off debts is more comfortable than bathing in Tangshan.

Looking at the sword in the middle of the night is the behavior of a knight-errant; endlessly chanting poetry is the true nature of a poet.

Seeing the fields and villages from the Suzhou-Shanghai train, I want to take off my dusty clothes and change into a summer shirt.

Mei Lanfang's Visit to Deputy Commander Zhang in Nanjing 171

— Yijun

Mei Lanfang and his entourage arrived in Shanghai on the 24th of this month by the first train from Tianjin to Nanjing, as reported in various newspapers. The day before he left from Beiping, he received a telegram from a friend in Nanjing saying that Deputy Commander Zhang wanted to meet Mei when he passed through Nanjing. Mei immediately telegraphed back that it was possible. When the train arrived in Pu on the morning of the 26th, more than a dozen of Mei's friends, including Shu Shifu, who is currently serving as a military advisor in the National Government, greeted him at the station. Mei immediately boarded a special ferry with his secretary Li Feishu, Da Wutai manager Huang Quansheng, and the welcoming guests. The others who came with him went directly to Shanghai by car. After Mei and others arrived in Nanjing, they first went to Shu's residence for a short rest. The mayor of Nanjing, Wei Daoming, had already received the news of Mei's arrival in Nanjing and immediately held a banquet at his private residence to welcome Mei. Mei then went to the banquet, and those present included Li Shizeng and Peng Huaiyu. Director Peng came with Deputy Commander Zhang this time. Mei then asked him when the Deputy Commander would be available. Peng telegraphed the headquarters and was told that Mei was invited to go at 2 PM. It was already past 1 PM. After a hurried banquet, he went directly to the Deputy Commander's headquarters with Li Feishu, accompanied by Tian Shijie and Shu Shifu, two military advisors from the National Government. Inside and outside the headquarters, sentries were posted everywhere, and the security was extremely strict. Mei's car should have driven directly inside, and the soldiers all raised their guns to salute. After the aide submitted the visiting card, the Deputy Commander came out to see him in a few minutes, stepped forward to shake hands with Mei, and said to Mei, "I haven't seen you for a long time. This trip to the United States was very hard. I read the newspaper and knew that you were praised by the people there, which is a glory for the country." Mei was humble and unassuming. Mei then introduced the people who came with him, and they took their seats. Zhang said, "The other day, my wife came and said that she met you in Tianjin. I also wanted to know the details of your visit to the United States and wanted to see you." Mei then presented a detailed account of his experience in the United States. Zhang was encouraging and urged Mei to work hard. He also asked Mei how many days he would be in Shanghai. Mei replied that it would be about a month and a half. After that, he might come to Nanjing again. Mei also asked the Deputy Commander when he would return to the north and whether he would go to Beiping. Zhang said that he might be able to go to Beiping in four or five days, but it was not yet decided whether to go to Beiping or return directly to Liaoning. By the time he finished speaking, it was already almost 4 PM. Zhang had to attend a transportation conference, so Mei and others said goodbye and went with Shu and Li to visit Ming Mausoleum and pay their respects to Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum. The mausoleum gate was already closed. Mei stood at the gate and bowed three times to show his respect. He then returned to Shu's residence to rest. At 7 PM, he went to the banquet at Mayor Wei's house. Li Shizeng's banquet also discussed in detail the improvement of drama and the fundraising for the Chinese Conservatory of Music. Zhang was supposed to attend the banquet, but he was afraid that he would not be able to come until after 10 PM because he was attending Jiang Jieshi's banquet. Mei had to take the 11 PM train to Shanghai, so he did not wait long and said goodbye to the host and went to the Xiaguan station. When the train passed through Zhongshan Avenue, Mei greatly admired the perfection and neatness of the road, saying that it was very similar to the rural roads in the United States. After arriving at the station, he immediately boarded the train. The train car was reserved by Mr. Li Shizeng, who specially gave it to Mei. The train left at 11 PM and arrived in Shanghai at 7 AM the next morning, going directly to the Fanwang Temple to stay. When the reporter visited Mei yesterday, Mei was out on business. I met Mr. Li Feishu, whom I had met before. He was writing a letter to a friend in Beiping, reporting his visit to Zhang in Nanjing, and showed it to me. I silently remembered his words and wrote this.

Jiaotong University and Guanghua University Mandarin Debate Record of Interest 172

— Zhizheng

After the Four Universities English Speech Contest was completed, there was also a Mandarin debate. The debaters used the same topic to divide into positive and negative sides, each refuting the other with reasons. Therefore, it was more interesting than a speech. On the afternoon of the 26th, Jiaotong University and Guanghua University held a preliminary competition. The venue was the Wenzhi Hall of Jiaotong University. Before 3 PM, it was already crowded with people. Now I will choose to record some trivia to fill this talk.

One Chinese and One Western: The meeting started at 4 PM. The president of Jiaotong University, Li Zhaohuan, presided over the meeting. The debaters occupied both sides of the rostrum. Each school had three representatives. The Guanghua representatives were all wearing Chinese-style robes, while Jiaotong University was all wearing black suits. One Chinese and one Western complemented each other, which was also a fun thing.

Sharp Words: The six representatives took turns to state their reasons in order. The topic of the debate that day was (Shanghai universities should be merged into a large-scale university) (Jiaotong University advocated the positive side, and Guanghua University advocated the negative side. Both sides had very sufficient reasons. The general idea of the positive side was that the times needed it, and it saved expenses. The negative side argued that each school had its own special relationship, and their natures were different. How could they be mixed together?) The words were sharp, and the listeners felt unparalleled interest and forgot their fatigue.

Wonderful Refutation: After the six representatives finished their speeches, they rested for five minutes and then began the refutation. The refuters collected the other side's reasons and refuted them item by item. It was very difficult because it was out of the blue and only lasted five minutes. Liu Xuantian from Jiaotong University refuted each point of Guanghua based on his talent, making the other side completely devastated. The wonderful performance caused cheers to thunder. For example, Guanghua said that universities should not be limited to national and established ones. Private schools should also be included. However, Jiaotong University said that those that have not been established have lost their legal qualifications, so they cannot be considered universities, and so on. The back-and-forth of the words was very audible.

The Chairman Encouraged Female Students to Join: After the refutation, the judges Zhu Shaoping, Gui Zhongshu, Chen Heqin, etc., calculated the scores. The chairman took the opportunity to report on the history and benefits of the debate and said that female students had joined the English speech, but there was no Mandarin debate, which was a pity. He hoped that it would not be the case next year so that the listeners would feel more enjoyable.

Amazing Charts: For the sake of fully increasing its strength, Jiaotong University specially drew many charts, such as student comparison charts for each university, economic status competition charts, etc., all more than a dozen colorful and exquisitely drawn. It was indeed the magic weapon for winning this time. It can be said that a lot of effort was put into it.

Jiaotong University's Double Happiness: Before long, the chairman announced the results. The first place individual was Liu Xuantian from Jiaotong University, who won a silver medal. The first place group belonged to the positive side, so it was also won by Jiaotong University. It can be said that double happiness came to the door. For a time, cheers shook the house. It was indeed a grand event.

Ming's Linguistic Repentance: In addition to Liu, the Jiaotong University representative also included China's delegation leader to the Far Eastern Games, the discus king Ming Jun. Because Jun was unable to fully prepare due to work, the result was ranked sixth (sixth place) and Yiming. The linguistic repentance also happened to be a coincidence, so it was attached to it.

The Rural Carnival at Shanghai University: A Postscript 173

— Du Zhaoshu

On the sixty-fifth anniversary of the birth of the late Mr. Sun Yat-sen, our school celebrated with a special Rural Carnival. On this day, the sky was clear, and the traffic on the banks of the Huangpu River was extremely heavy. Zhaoshu personally attended the grand event and was happy. Therefore, I recorded its brief outline as follows:

The Grand Occasion of the Venue: The center of the conference was in Yates Hall. The slogans were fresh and full of beautiful things, reflecting the yellow and purple chrysanthemums listed on all sides, especially for the education, health, agriculture, industry and commerce exhibitions listed on the upper floors, mainly to open up the knowledge of the rural people. The most exciting of its various pastimes are Tan Xiaolin's erhu, Wu Tiesheng's unicycle show, the national music society's music, and the science museum's movies, all of which can make rural people dance and be happy.

The Attention-Grabbing of the Female Dormitory: The Japanese school girls' dormitory is open, and the furnishings are more simple, such as a certain room with a white wall lining a white bed, or a certain piece of goods with a uniform goose yellow, all of which can attract people's attention. Some university students who visited sighed and said, "It's amazing!" It is so moving to the eye.

The Fun of Arguing Over the Ding: In the middle school student achievement exhibition, there were paper and wax fruits. The villagers thought it was real and applauded, saying that the students were affectionate and gave us fruits. After looking at it for a long time, they smiled and stopped. When Principal's wife Ms. Wang distributed hundreds of bags of candy to the children of the villagers, the elders also competed for it. When the Sanyou Industrial Company gave national goods towels, the villagers' new clothes and hats were sacrificed a lot because they were too crowded and their hats fell off and their clothes were torn. In particular, arguing over the ding was interesting and showed the ingenuity of the operation, which added to the glory of the conference.

The Wonderful Football Match: In the morning, the university football team of our school competed with Guanghua. Hu Minteng performed the best in our school. The rest, such as Huang Jiaoyan and Zhao Xitian, also had considerable performances. The inside guards of Guanghua were all good, and the rest were also competent. It is a pity that I cannot mention their names. In the afternoon, the middle school of our school competed with St. John's Middle School. Among them, Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang were the best. They were wearing white clothes and white pants and had smiling faces. Although they had wins and losses, they did not care at all. Their spirit of friendship was admirable. Finally, the basketball game between Huadong and the middle school of our school was also wonderful.

The Busy Support of the Head of Our Regiment: On this day, the order in the school was maintained by our Boy Scouts. The head of the regiment, Ni Jiaxi, also served as the reception director. He had to inspect our negligence from time to time, and he had to go back and forth to entertain the guests and guide the villagers to visit. His busy support was like this.

Travel Notes from Southeast Asia (89) 174

— Linghua

On the fifth day, the Daoist came and said that he had a dream that night. Guanyin spoke to him and showed him the red kasaya he was wearing, saying, "This is made of human flesh." The inner layer of blue kasaya said, "This is made of animal flesh." Another layer of kasaya said, "This is made of the flesh of different kinds of beings." After saying that, he said, "I am going to see God to discuss the method of saving the world." Then he held the incense burner and flew into the air. I responded indifferently. In the afternoon, Master Wan came and said that Professor Liu Tianxi of Yangon University had invited him to tea. So, we went together and visited his school outside the big lake. Students were practicing swimming. There were Eastern and Western Document Rooms in the school. Master Dao entered the Western Document Room and saw colored Dunhuang Stone Chamber Buddhist scriptures and Buddha statues printed in London. When he opened it for the first time, he saw a Tang Dynasty painting of Guanyin in red. Master Dao said, "This is exactly the same as what I dreamed of at night." He also saw a blue-clothed Guanyin statue, which was also the same as the dream. It is said that dreams often foretell the future, which is the so-called way to communicate day and night.

On the evening of the sixth day, a sermon was held in Myanmar to save the world from Eastern culture, which was very welcome. The meeting was hosted by Indians. The leader was a female teacher, Dri Beansang, also known as Bisheng. It is said that there are 15 million people worldwide, and Shanghai also has its location, one at the east end of Damalu and one at the intersection of Kade Road on Jing'an Temple Road. A girls' school is run there. I often go there. In the past, Mr. Wu Tingfang joined its meeting. Master Wan said that it was founded by a Russian woman dozens of years ago. Russia wanted to plot against Tibet and sent people to learn Tibetan Buddhism. There are secret magic powers. The Russian woman did not return to Russia but preached in India. The female leader has died, and there are two male and female disciples. The man is named Dharmapala, and the woman is Bisheng. The woman has magic powers, but the man does not, but both can manage property, so they are quite attached to by the general public. The church is scattered everywhere and is prosperous in India. If it is in India, it will not dare to slander it. If it is slandered, it will be dominated by its power. According to the purpose it has announced, it is for the world peace movement, but according to Master Wan, its doctrine is also lofty, and it is also extremely advocating for the freedom of men and women. However, it does not advocate fertility. Indians often have secret skills. According to its members, Bisheng is nearly sixty years old and is now going to England to show me her image, which is now called the Mother of the World. When I come to India, I will definitely visit its meeting.

Warmth in the Heart (327) 175

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Sixteen: Cui Xiu Earnestly Asks for Guidance from the Teacher, Generous Talk of Military Affairs and a Feast for Heroines in a Brothel

Thereupon, the few people swayed and swaggered to the Xinghua Restaurant. Fortunately, although snowflakes were dancing, they were not very heavy. As they walked through the glass doors of the Xinghua Restaurant, they immediately felt as if spring had filled the room and it was much warmer. As they stepped onto the escalator, a waiter behind the counter uttered a sound without discernible meaning, and no one knew what he was saying. Guessing from his intent, he was probably calling out to welcome the guests, alerting the waiters upstairs to pay attention. Two or three waiters were already waiting on the stairs, all wearing uniforms made of blue wool, with two red Roman numerals on their chests, which were their assigned numbers, and a pencil clipped to their ears. The waiters in the Cantonese restaurants seemed neater than those in other restaurants. They led them to a room facing west along the road, which was quite spacious. Ye Haoran wanted to change to another room, as he found this place too noisy and preferred somewhere quieter. However, the waiter said that there were no other rooms available, except for this one. It turned out that next door was a hall where a wealthy family was hosting a large banquet, calling for countless Cantonese prostitutes and a band of musicians. There were loud sounds of gongs, drums, and cymbals, creating a deafening noise. Whenever Cantonese people host a large banquet, known as "opening the hall," they always have Cantonese prostitutes and a band of musicians to make a lot of noise. Ye Haoran wanted to change the location because he found it too noisy, which was why. Ling Zhixiang said, "Let them make noise. We can make noise too. They can call Cantonese opera singers, and we can call local opera singers." Long Ziyun said, "No matter what, we can't outdo them in making noise. The opera singers we call can only sing Kunqu opera with the accompaniment of the erhu, pipa, and a flute. They have gongs and drums like the heavens are falling, and there's also something like the clapper in Northern Bangzi opera. I don't know what it is. In their symphony, there's a cymbal as big as a shield, and you can imagine how loud the sound is. One day, a Cantonese friend invited me to Hongkou to see Cantonese opera, saying that two famous Cantonese performers had just arrived from Hong Kong and were said to sing very well. That Cantonese friend knew the plot of the opera and could understand their lyrics, nodding and enjoying himself immensely. But I felt completely clueless. The strangest thing was that their stage also had a group of people playing gongs and drums, making music. In Peking opera, this is called the 'changmian.' The performers only sing, and the 'changmian' people never open their mouths. But in Cantonese opera, the 'changmian' people sing along with the actors. Sometimes, during chaotic dancing, the 'changmian' people hold up two large cymbals and dance wildly along with the actors. This is truly laughable to see." In the middle of their conversation, they heard a burst of zheng and clanging sounds from next door, which turned out to be the Cantonese prostitutes playing the dulcimer. Soon after, they heard a melodious singing voice. Long Ziyun said, "This is probably a 'qingshan' from the Cantonese opera."

Business News: Financial Gold Market Soars Straight Up

Soaring Seven Taels and One Mace

Future Prospects Remain Optimistic

Rapid Strides Forward, Peaks Repeatedly Appear. Yesterday, December 2nd, the price of gold repeatedly reached new peaks, once again exceeding the 600 tael mark, advancing swiftly as if about to reach the summit. However, the daily total turnover was only four taels, with minor fluctuations. Purchases and sales varied greatly among dealers, each acting according to their own intentions. The foreign exchange rate continued to decrease by half a cent, but the domestic market remained strong, with eager buyers. As for over-the-counter transactions, dealers such as Yuansheng, Yuanmao, and Yongyu were actively buying, while Lianbang and Fuchang, Taiheng Yuan, etc., were still actively selling. The overseas silver market experienced a sharp decline, with strong selling intentions from the United States. Therefore, even after a rapid surge, sellers did not relent, leading to a sudden downturn. The price dropped from over 603 taels to just over 600 taels. The future market is expected to be strong due to the favorable exchange rate, and the buying momentum from Taitai Chang, Wanxing Shunli, Yu Da, and others in the market is strong, leading to a remarkable surge in prices. A new peak of 604 taels and six mace was reached, with fluctuations of only one tael or so. Automobile News

Commentary

Diesel Car Success, Chan Sent from England 193

The development of the automobile industry is faster than any other means of transportation, advancing a thousand miles a day and sweeping the globe. In a few decades, it has become an important issue in transportation. However, the gasoline used (commonly known as petrol) is very expensive. In the past ten years, the diesel engine has made rapid progress, and major power plants around the world have gradually switched to diesel engines. The latest trains have also adopted diesel engines, but their use in automobiles is still limited. According to a recent report from the British automotive industry, diesel cars have been successful, saving fuel, being durable, and setting new records in automotive engineering. Newspapers praised and celebrated the event across the country. In recent years, highways have been built in various provinces of China, and the annual consumption of fuel is considerable. If diesel engines can be used instead, up to one-sixth of the cost can be saved. I have translated the details of each car for your reference.

(1) Wardman Five-Seater car: This car has a ten-horsepower diesel engine installed in a typical five-seater car body. The engine shaft speed ranges from 200 to 1,200 revolutions per minute. The car's top speed is 20 miles per hour. A month ago, it was tested between London and Brighton, a round trip of 112 miles, consuming less than two gallons of fuel (British price is five pence per gallon, and each penny equals seven fen in national currency), costing nine pence, which can be considered extremely cheap. The previously mentioned difficulties of "Heavy Weight" and "High Compression" have been overcome, and the combustion is complete, with cleaner exhaust than gasoline. There is also a device for easy starting, without the need for a Magneto, Induction Coil, spark Plug, and Carburator. The igniter and mixer are the most easily damaged parts of a car, so the diesel engine car's parts are simple and easy to manage.

(2) Gardner type diesel bus: This car was manufactured by Crossley Motor Company, Manchester, using a Kai's (phonetic) diesel engine installed in a double-decker bus with 80 horsepower. It has traveled 30,000 miles without any damage. The test results were very perfect. The required fuel price is only one-sixth of ordinary gasoline. The diesel fuel consumption is only one-third, but the efficiency is doubled. The Economical Effecien reaches over 80 percent. Each hundred miles only requires a fuel cost of two shillings and seven pence. If gasoline were used, it would cost sixteen shillings and six pence. This car can accommodate 48 passengers and travel 40 miles per hour.

(3) Laffley lorry: This car also uses a diesel engine and carries four tons of gravel. It traveled 192 miles from Manchester to London in four hours and forty-eight minutes, consuming 9.75 gallons of fuel. The price per gallon was 5.5 pence, costing a total of four shillings and six pence. Its average speed was 21.8 miles per hour. This is a successful heavy-duty vehicle. Overall, the aforementioned diesel cars have become an important issue in the transportation industry. The ignition point of diesel is very high, unlike gasoline which is easy to ignite. The fuel storage is also safer. The exhaust after combustion does not have the odor of gasoline and contains less toxic gas. Starting the car is very easy, and the horsepower is sufficient. All of this is enough to surpass ordinary cars. As for the engineering advantages, due to space limitations, I cannot describe them in detail. I will discuss them later.

1931 Morris Car 194

The 1931 Morris new car is now on display at Liham Machine Automobile Company, 694 Jing'an Temple Road. Its harmonious and beautiful colors, excellent style, and great utility are all captivating. As for its economic efficiency, safety, reliability, and various mechanical features, it is an unprecedented great contribution to the British automobile industry. The new car is divided into five groups, with various sizes and prices to suit the needs of people from all walks of life. Those who purchase it will find it exactly what they are looking for and will be satisfied.

There are three types of six-cylinder Morris new cars: Morris Major, Morris Cowley, and Morris Essex. There are two types of four-cylinder cars: Morris Minor and Morris Oxford. The horsepower of these models ranges from eight to eighteen. There are a total of eighteen types of car bodies, among which the Morris Minor sports car is the most worthy of mention, as its price is particularly low and truly surprising.

The Morris Major has 15 horsepower and six cylinders. The Cowley engine has been specially improved to increase horsepower and acceleration. The Cowley body and other parts have been refined to perfection. The Essex has 18 horsepower and is equipped with various new devices such as air purifiers and preheaters. Among the advantages of the new Morris car, the biggest one is the step-by-step lubrication method, which provides thorough lubrication without neglect, so its utility is greater and more durable.

Broadway Truck and Long-Distance Bus 195

— Ji

Solid construction, completely new, reduced transportation costs, fast and durable.

Today's cargo transportation tools must adapt to the ever-changing transportation needs of today. Old profitable trucks have been abandoned as waste by the current world.

The new Broadway 120 truck and long-distance bus are designed to meet the urgent needs of modern transportation. The new style and new products do not prevent comparison with other cars and are not old cars with new tires. The body structure is completely based on new ideas and the application of specialized knowledge to create a truck suitable for today.

Not only that, but all Broadway trucks have been inspected by experts and proven to be solid and reliable, and have been sold only after passing thousands of miles of vigorous testing with excellent results, so car owners trust them. In places with complex car affairs, rural transportation, and long-distance travel, the Broadway 120 truck can handle heavy loads.

Because of the solid construction and uniform mechanical power, it is durable and guarantees long-term service, reducing all costs. The powerful and sensitive motor generates fast speed and divine power, avoiding accidental dangers. The strong four-speed power transmission expands the driving range and adapts to various car affairs conditions. The rear axle is a fully floating single-cover low-drop helical bevel type, with large pointed wheels and a smooth surface.

Not only is the action excellent, but the appearance is also very outstanding. The style of the 120 truck is novel, and you will want to order it as soon as you see it. This kind of amazing vehicle has powerful capabilities and can handle various weights. With this truck, you can serve day and night, quickly, properly, and accurately. Broadway 120 is the most perfect truck and the most economical transportation tool of today.

The engine is mounted on four suspension points, so the hub is more stable. The crossbars on the three heavier wheelbases are equipped with double-acting shock absorbers, which minimize restraint and vibration. The extra-long semi-elliptical springs have been improved. The new spring shock absorbers and the underpan work together, so the quietness of the road and the comfort of driving and riding of Buick cars, even at the highest speed, cannot be surpassed by other cars.

The style of the low chassis is refreshing, and the car's chain hooks are simple and strong, eliminating the previous cumbersome procedures. The driving gears, spring chain hooks, and car body all have brackets and pillars with widths equal to the depth of the crossbars to ensure sufficient supporting force.

The 8-50 low chassis is shorter and lighter than the 8-60, 8-80, and 8-90, but its effectiveness is equal to that of the large low chassis. These types of cars are equipped with a (Hua Qie Ke Si) driver and single shock absorber.

Book Review

Outline of Imperialist Colonial Policy 199

— Tang Bin

Authored by Hu Shiming

Colonial policy is not only an extremely important part of politics but also the most significant issue in the world today. The Chinese people, living in a semi-colonial state, need to study this issue in detail. However, we must understand that behind modern colonial policy lies a terrifying picture of humanity, not a portrait of civilizational progress. It can be described as a bloody and chaotic painting filled with brutality, misery, weeping, and death, arousing both fear and indignation. This is a very obvious fact. We only need to look at the real lives of the Indian, Vietnamese, and Korean peoples to understand the true nature of colonial policy. Generally speaking, the people in colonies are treated worse than slaves, cattle, or fish; their lives and deaths are entirely at the mercy of the imperialists. As colonial policy becomes more aggressive, the fate of weak nations becomes more tragic. Even in our semi-colonial China, these so-called tragic realities can be seen at any time and any place. Indeed, colonial policy not only fails to promote the spread of civilization but also hinders culture and destroys humanity everywhere.

Regarding books on colonial policy, especially those with correct perspectives and centered on national consciousness, there are very few in Chinese publications. The purpose of this book by Mr. Hu is to enable the Chinese people to understand the true nature and actual situation of imperialist colonial policy. Therefore, it analyzes and explores in detail the reasons for imperialists' implementation of colonial policy and its inner workings. This is not only helpful for those studying politics and international issues but also provides the people of semi-colonial countries with the common knowledge they should have. The book is divided into eight chapters: (1) Introduction, (2) Classification of Colonies, (3) Origins of Modern Colonial Policy, (4) Imperialist Aims in Seizing Colonies, (5) Organization and Forms of Colonial Rule, (6) Imperialist Policies for Ruling Colonies, (7) Brief History of Modern Imperialist Colonialism, and (8) Conclusion. Finally, there is an appendix (Investigation of Colonies of Various Imperialist Countries in Recent Times), which is particularly detailed and valuable.

In the introduction, the author objectively explains the elements of imperialism and its past and present external aggression. It systematically discusses from ancient times to modern times, such as the external aggressions of Assyria and Babylon in the ancient East, the actual situation of Spanish and Portuguese colonial management at the beginning of the fifteenth century, and the fact that England became the world's largest colonial country after Spain. At the very least, it gives us a holistic and systematic understanding of the history of colonialism.

The author classifies colonies according to scientific methods, detailing how the policies adopted by various countries towards colonies differ and pointing out their characteristics. For example, the British divide colonies according to political organization into Crown Colonies and Self-Governing Colonies. Those directly under the rule of the Governor, who is subordinate to the British monarch, are called Crown Colonies. Hong Kong and the Straits Settlements belong to this category. Colonies with a constitution, a nominally self-governing system, and a parliament and officials elected by elections are called Self-Governing Colonies. Canada and the South African Union belong to this category. However, the author wants readers to see the characteristics of colonies and colonial policy by focusing on important aspects. Therefore, in addition to this classification, it is classified based on political conditions: (A) Independent Colonies, (B) Protectorates, (C) Leased Territories, and (D) Spheres of Influence. Each category has a detailed explanation based on the country to which the colony belongs. Secondly, it is classified based on economic conditions: (A) Settlement Colonies, (B) Trading Colonies, (C) Commercial Colonies, (D) Plantation Colonies, and (E) Military Colonies. The author's classification is profoundly meaningful and reasonable.

The driving force of modern colonial policy explores the main and secondary reasons for the vigorous implementation of colonial policy by modern imperialism, such as population growth, transportation development, military expansion, Christian propagation, and the activities of explorers. The last one, such as the Russians in Abyssinia and the British in Tibet, all use scientific investigation as a pretext for reconnaissance, which are extremely obvious facts.

The purpose of imperialist seizure of colonies explains what its purpose is, why it wants to invade colonies, and what benefits it has for itself. The author has detailed analyses of these major issues.

The organization and form of colonial rule: (1) The doctrine of governing colonies differs due to the circumstances and needs of each country. According to the author's research, it is divided into four types: (A) Assimilationism, (B) Autonomism, (C) Centralism, and (D) Distributionism. (2) The organization of colonial rule is roughly divided into three types of institutions: (A) Governing institutions in the mother country, (B) Governing institutions in the colony, and (C) Colonial companies. (3) The form of colonial rule varies depending on the circumstances of each country, so there are also some differences in various forms, but they can also be roughly divided into four types: (A) Protected Colony, (B) Chartered Colony, (C) Directly Ruled Colony, and (D) Autonomously Ruled Colony. The author has unique insights into each organization and form, which is worth our attention.

The author details the complex content of the imperialist policy of ruling colonies: (1) Political policies, (2) Financial policies, (3) Industrial policies, (4) Transportation policies, and (5) Policies towards scholars. These are all elaborated, allowing readers to understand the actual situation and are a very important chapter.

A brief history of modern imperialist colonies describes the earliest European countries engaged in colonial undertakings in order, such as the colonial history of Spain and Portugal, the colonial history of the Netherlands, and the colonial history of England. In Australia, it covers the colonization of New Zealand and Western Australia, among others. Secondly, it details the colonial history of France in North America, Italy, Japan, and the United States.

In short, the author's book is based on a modern perspective to analyze imperialist colonial policy. In other words, it is to awaken the weak nations of various countries. Of course, the people in the colonies themselves have long felt the pain. Although the entire book has only eight chapters, it comprehensively describes the origins, purposes, and content of colonial policy, as well as a brief history of the implementation of colonial policy by various imperialist countries, and its important aspects are all described without omission. The detailed investigation of the colonies of various imperialist countries at the end is sufficient for researchers to refer to. Sun Yat-sen has already said in the Three Principles of the People that our China has become a semi-colonial country, so we need to study this imperialist colonial policy even more. When there are few such books published in the country, Mr. Hu's book is worth recommending to readers.

[P Baoshan People

— Wang Tiehua

Edited by the Baoshan People's Education Center

The so-called nation naturally refers to all its members, and definitely not just the intellectuals of the nation. Therefore, the literature and art produced in a certain nation do not only refer to the works produced by intellectuals from their individual consciousness, but rather refer to the works produced from the life consciousness formed from the standpoint of the nation, and their value is estimated. This kind of folk heritage cannot be ignored.

In the past, this newspaper has introduced many books and newspapers about folk tales, folk legends, folk songs, etc. This kind of national art is indeed worthy of attention and recommendation to the public. Therefore, I dare to present "Baoshan People" for introduction.

"Baoshan People" is a bi-monthly publication edited by the Baoshan County People's Education Center. It has been working tirelessly for almost two years. Needless to say, the content is very rich. Fortunately, it can use simple writing to express sincere meanings and instill them into the general public. Each issue has short essays, anecdotes, news, songs, creations, etc., which are adjusted so that it does not feel boring or monotonous. What is most worthy of our attention is that many folk songs have been discovered here. At the same time, there are also many excellent works of short song creation and adaptation dedicated to the "people." Here are a few excerpts:

(Little chicken, yellow all over, which daughter doesn't miss her mother? When she misses her mother, there's nowhere to go, so she closes the door and cries. Although my parents-in-law treat me well, it's not as good as my own parents.)

(Eating doesn't make you poor, dressing doesn't make you poor, miscalculation makes you poor for life. I advise you to look at Fang Taigong in Nan Village. His calculation is the most accurate. The father-in-law carries burdens to sell yellow onions himself, and the mother-in-law can also cut bamboo to make lanterns. The eldest son does massage as a doctor, and the youngest son learns tailoring on Nan Village Street. The daughters-in-law spin yarn and weave cloth as female workers. Do you think his calculation is accurate? I advise everyone to look at Fang Taigong in Nan Village.)

The first song probably refers to a newly married woman, and the second vividly depicts a simple life in the countryside.

At the same time, Mr. Zhu Yunzong, the author of many songs and dramas, has put in a lot of effort to use historical sites to make songs about the four seasons, using a language that the general public can understand to narrate an event, pretending to use popular folk songs to promote the consciousness of (avenging shame). This kind of work is naturally much greater than humming a few sentences of (Bright Moon and Gentle Breeze) and singing a few sentences of (Sister, I Love You).

Each "Four Seasons Mountain Song" has some (introduction) in front to make it easier for people to understand the facts. Now I excerpt a few sentences below:

In addition, topics such as (province) and (county) can also give the public geographical and historical knowledge. Here is a song about (Baoshan County):

In spring, the plum blossoms are fragrant, Baoshan County is in the northern boundary of Jiangsu Province, south of Taicang, east of Shanghai, and west of the sea is Jiading. In summer, lotus flowers are full of ponds, the fields in Baoshan have been measured, and the area is more than 370,000 mu, a flat and good place. In autumn, osmanthus flowers are like gold, Baoshan County is divided into five districts, and each district has a district chief to handle affairs for the people. In winter, snowflakes are as white as cotton, Baoshan has a population of 160,000, everyone works hard to make progress, and will become a model county in the future. There are already many excerpts of songs, and I am afraid that panic will occur in the position, so I have to turn to other aspects.

We know that people's gatherings and entertainment are mixed with many feudal and superstitious ideas on the one hand, and also contain a very strong national spirit on the other hand. For this kind of group action, such as welcoming gods and holding temple fairs, dragon boat racing, singing flower drum operas, improper entertainment, etc., naturally cannot be absolutely prevented in (Baoshan), and their actions may not have enthusiastic expressions of feelings. The expression of group consciousness, organized actions, and active and vivid states are not inconsistent with the national spirit, so they should not be subject to negative prohibition. It is urgent to sort out and correct their consciousness and give play to it, turning the unconscious into conscious, which is indeed an important event in various places at present. There are also many discussions on this point in the publication.

In short, "Baoshan People" speaks for the people from the standpoint of the people and speaks to the people. At this time when (people's education) is in urgent need of popularization, the publication has a major responsibility and is worthy of recommendation and attention. At the same time, it is hoped that folk literature will be collected more, and such works with the purpose of seeking survival, freedom, and prosperity for the nation should be regarded as the treasure of national art and cannot be ignored.

Youth Corner

Establishment of the Guangming (Brightness) Academic Society at the Faculty of Law and Politics 200

— Wen

This semester, the organization of academic groups at the Faculty of Law and Politics has been quite active, and the Guangming Academic Society is particularly outstanding. However, in the past, we have not heard of the organization of the Guangming Academic Society. It is very gratifying to read the Guangming Bi-Monthly Publication, which is about to reach its third issue. Most students have expressed welcome and praise, which has aroused the sympathy of some people and a tendency to request to participate in joint efforts. Unexpectedly, the person in charge of the society is also very generous. Since it is difficult to refuse their sincerity, they agreed to become a tangible organization and openly solicit members. In total, more than 100 people have joined, which is truly the beginning of a new era. At 7:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, their inaugural meeting was held in the first classroom. The attendees were unusually crowded and all expressed their sincere attitude, so the spiritual nourishment was constant and persistent, which is truly admirable. In particular, although the general female students were shy and rarely spoke, I believe that their seriousness about the proposals and elections was all inspired by their inner selves and added a lot of color. Zhu Jianbai, Cao Huichuan, and Ms. Guo Shiying were immediately elected as the presidium. After the ceremony, Chairman Zhu Jianbai gave a report, which was roughly like this:

………In the past, our Guangming was an unorganized one. The Guangming Bi-Monthly Publication was also only responsible for by a few of us with similar interests. Initially, our motivation for launching it was also to feel the dangerous phenomenon in the entire youth world. This kind of stimulation made us uncover the inner depression and form the task of having to stand up to save. From all aspects, we observed that the performance of the current youth world everywhere reveals a state of being inferior. Because the will of young people is weak, they are easily trapped in an irredeemable situation. The Communist Party is recklessly instigating and creating one riot after another, and I don’t know how many young people with burning blood have been sacrificed. The Nationalists are insidiously anesthetizing, and I don’t know how many young people are having sleeping lion dreams, not only not moving forward but also going backward, even to the point of digging their own graves. At the same time, the so-called decadence and romance not only do not know to be ashamed but are staggering and proud. What kind of impact will such degeneration have on the future of national life? As for the cultural aspect, the Communist Party members are also using the two major strategies of the social science movement and the literary movement to desperately launch a chain offensive against us. When they talk about social science, they vigorously promote their radicalism, such as Marx and Kautsky. When they write literary works, they vigorously advocate class struggle, such as hunger, poverty, and ruin. Because young people do not have a central idea, they are often infected by it. Moreover, we also admit that the silence in the youth world is indeed not without reason. However, if we want to break the atmosphere of silence and replace it with a new situation, we must break that crisis. Therefore, we want to fulfill the responsibility of exploring the youth problem. In the youth's thinking, we have gained deep understanding and reflection. We should work hard on the anti-Marxist social science movement to avoid the general public from taking the wrong revolutionary path. Secondly, we should work hard on the nationalist literary movement, passively resisting proletarian literature and actively arousing national consciousness and promoting the realization of nationalism, in order to achieve the goal of freedom and equality for the entire nation. In terms of action, how can we eliminate the youth's morbidity and lead them to the bright path of upward, brave, creative, and revolutionary. Therefore, we first issued the Guangming Bi-Monthly Publication beyond our capacity, and recently we clearly organized our Guangming Academic Society. We are willing to advance on the predetermined path and pursue everything we want to pursue under the illumination of Guangming…

After the Chairman's report, the proposals were discussed and passed: (1) The Society should organize a tour group to broaden their knowledge. (2) The Society should organize a visiting group to visit various political groups and institutions. (3) Compile a roster of members. (4) Issue a declaration in the name of the General Assembly. (5) Expand the Guangming Bi-Monthly Publication into a booklet and change it to a monthly publication. The election results were as follows: Zhu Airen, Ms. Guo Shiying, Wu Wanbang, Li Erbai, Gu Yufei, Cao Huichuan, Mei Hongquan, Zhou Hanbin, Lu Jinsong, Ms. Xie Huichang, Ms. Chen Naizhi, Li Chunsen, Li Zheng, Lu Wei, and Ms. Wei Zhiping were elected as directors. Ms. Li Suzhen, Feng Guanjun, Wu Weicai, Ms. Ge Cairong, and Zhang Xiaorong were elected as alternates.

By the time the meeting adjourned, it was already 11:00 p.m. Everyone was bathed in the cold air and called out, "See you tomorrow!"

Crossroads 201

— Zhengtian

When I left Changsha for Shanghai, Zhujun put two dollars in my pocket and said to me:

(I want to start oil painting this semester. I can’t buy paintbrushes here, so please take the trouble to buy six paintbrushes for me. If the money is not enough, please pay for me a little and I will return it to you later. I am waiting to use them, so please be quick.)

(Okay, I'll buy them for you when I get to Shanghai.)

Shanghai arrived, one day, two days, three days, one week, two weeks, three weeks, the brushes are still in the stationery store. Friend, it's not that I forgot, but two dollars is not enough to buy six oil paintbrushes, not to mention that I have spent even the two dollars. I am anxious every day because I am sorry for you, but what can I do? Even if I use my personality as a guarantee, the stationery store will not sell the brushes on credit.

The airmail has arrived again for two days. Before I even opened it, I knew it was to urge me to buy the brushes. If I don't get a few dollars today, your telegram will arrive, won't it? Are you eager to indulge in oil painting, my friend?

The oil paintbrushes are probably cheaper at the Jincheng Arts & Crafts Society, I thought, so I went all the way from Tiantong'an to Avenue Dubail.

I had bought the brushes and it was already 5:30 p.m. Although I had to rush back for dinner, we walked from Xinxinli to Avenue Joffre because taking a rickshaw would cost twice as much as taking the tram from the French Concession to Hongkou.

It was already the world of electric lights. Avenue Joffre is a region where foreign powers flaunt their strength. Besides foreign food stores, foreign clothing stores, and foreign department stores, there are hardly any stores opened by Chinese people. Next to them are densely arranged rows of foreign parasol trees. In the middle, there are flowing cars and horses mixed with deafening noise. At that crossroads, there was a majestic, tall horse with a man sitting on it, watching the rushing people without moving, as if even a green fly on the street could not escape his eyes. An Annamese stood underneath, just as tall as the horse's body, looking up to the man on the horse's command.

Suddenly, the man on the horse raised his finger, and the man under the horse immediately ran to the middle and stopped an old Chinese rickshaw driver's rickshaw. Then he went to the back and took the license off the rickshaw and ran back to present the license to the man on the horse with both hands. He took it and just nodded.

The old rickshaw driver, that poor rickshaw driver, was probably in the dim electric light, his old eyes were dazzled and violated the rules by taking one step too far or retreating one step too far.

The old rickshaw driver just helplessly put the rickshaw on the side of the road, his pair of pitiful eyes looking at his passenger. He was lamenting his own bad fate. He could not think of any way out.

Suddenly, a bitter smile wrinkled on his withered face. He was asking his passenger to plead with the patrol officer for him. The passenger, who was carrying a large bundle, was also an old man like him. He sympathized with him and walked to the patrol officer, but the patrol officer's reply was just to shake his baton at him. So he quietly retreated.

The old passenger just stared blankly at his bundle.

The old rickshaw driver just stared blankly at his rickshaw that he could do nothing about.

The two of them had forgotten the noise around them.

Guidelines for Youth Corner Contributions 202

(1) The text should be related to the discussion of youth issues, news about domestic and foreign schools or students, essays, descriptions of school life, notes, etc. The style is not limited.

(2) Books are limited to those related to youth issues.

(3) Photos are qualified if they are about youth life (such as sports, travel, sightseeing, performing arts, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements, etc. Both individuals and groups are welcome.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) The number of words in each article should not exceed 2,000.

(6) Do not write manuscripts horizontally, and do not be sloppy. Western text can be omitted if possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink to draw pictures, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(8) Please indicate that the manuscripts should be sent to the Youth Corner Editorial Department.

(9) Whether the manuscripts are published or not, they will not be returned. If you need to return them, you should declare them in advance.

(10) The remuneration for written text is divided into three grades: three yuan, two yuan, and one yuan per thousand words. The remuneration for each picture and photo is the same. If there is a special manuscript, the remuneration will be calculated separately.

In this city, the publishing section of the News News Agency on Sanma Road, the Lixing Steamboat Bureau at Pentang Lane Bridge, and the Shida Store at the intersection of Xinzha Road and Changsha Road, Shuncheng Trust Bureau on Li Xian Gua Street outside Dadongmen, etc., all have sales agents so that patients can purchase and try them nearby.

Lianhua Woolen Mill, Hele Lane, North Henan Road, announced that the Three Wheels brand Western-style vests, sports shirts, men's and women's scarves, and woolen socks produced by this factory are extremely famous among domestic products. After the gold price soared, foreign goods became extremely expensive, and many Chinese people who used woolen products were happy to purchase products from this factory. Therefore, the business is becoming more and more prosperous, and orders are crowded and insufficient to meet the demand. Recently, a new-style motor worth nearly ten thousand yuan was added to speed up production.

Recently, Liming Bookstore, Dade Lane, South Chengdu Road, in view of the lack of university textbooks in China, has specially engaged in compiling a series of university lectures to meet the needs. It has now appointed Dai Ailu as the editor of the economics section and Wu Songgao and Sun Hanbing as the editors of the political science section. It is learned that two books in the economics section have been sent to print: (1) Recent Monetary and Financial Theories (translated by Dai Ailu) (2) Chinese Financial Theory (authored by Yang Yinpu). Both can be published within the year. It is also heard that the latest edition of Modern Political Thought History recently published by the bureau is a large volume jointly translated by Lu Guoxiang and Feng Hefa, and Sun Hanbing carefully revised it. The content and binding are extremely exquisite and the sales are very smooth.

Yonglinfeng Craft Society, Yipin Lane, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, Shanghai, announced that the envelopes issued by this society in service of the society have long been famous and are sought after by all walks of life. Recently, it has invented a kind of art flower envelopes, such as patriotic envelopes, international envelopes, rich and noble envelopes, love envelopes, etc. The business has developed exceptionally. Now, for the convenience of all walks of life, it has specially entrusted the Guanghua Printing Company at the intersection of Wangyun Lane, Hebei Road, near Paoliu Playground, as the distribution office.

The Oriental Dance Research Association in Yixin Lane, Laoyao Road, has been established for many years and has a large number of members. It can be called the oldest in terms of association qualifications. There are also not a few dance stars in various venues who have come out of its walls. Recently, it has also installed Vita-style music for guiding dance.

Theater News 204

The New World Amusement Park announced that since the 28th of last month, they have been holding a ten-day series of large-scale giveaways. For the past six days, the park has been crowded with visitors, and they have introduced various novel amusements, all of which are extremely rare skills. Such as the amazing artistry of the Flying Flying Troupe, and newly added variety dramas, which are very popular with the audience. In addition to sightseeing, there are also exquisite gifts, achieving two goals with one action. Therefore, those who go to visit are so numerous that there is no room to stand, it is said.

Medical News 205

The Foreign Women's Hospital (Chinic for women) at Route Larton, No. 131, French Concession, announced that the hospital has been open for years and has achieved considerable success. Now, it has newly hired specialized female doctors from Europe, Dr. Lakvorin-Faivshavilch and Dr. I. ll. Lguatov M.d., who specialize in treating all kinds of difficult and complicated diseases. The facilities are new and the service is thoughtful. Chinese ladies are welcome, and the fees are especially low, it is said.

German medical obstetrician and gynecologist Ms. Yu Qinfang specializes in treating leucorrhea in women, menstrual irregularities, amenorrhea, infertility, and all kinds of difficult and complicated prenatal and postpartum diseases, with remarkable effects. She has now set up a clinic at No. 7, the intersection of Shanhaiguan Road and Mei Baige Road. To facilitate patients, the original consultation hours have been extended to 10:00 am to 1:00 pm. The consultation fee is one dollar and twenty cents. The poor and sick will not be charged.
